Important Foreign Telegrams

Britain Confirms Holding General Election

Parliament to be Dissolved on the 7th of This Month

Government Platform Under Discussion

50,000 Unemployed Workers Demonstrate in Scotland

Looting of Shops Suppressed by Mounted Police

Reuters, London, News that a British general election has been confirmed, it is heard that the Prime Minister McDonald will ask the Emperor of Britain to dissolve the Parliament on October 7th, and the election will start on October 28th. Reuters learned today that five cabinet members of the Liberal Party, Samuel, Leadon, Sinclair, McLellan, and Lothian, secretly discussed several times and decided to support the National Government's election plan, knowing that the election is actually unavoidable. It is heard that McDonald, Baldwin and Samuel have agreed to submit the government platform to the election districts, including managing imported goods and adopting tax rates or other necessary methods to cope with the needs of the current financial situation. Other Liberal Party members who are working in the National Government will gather tomorrow to discuss the government platform.

Reuters, London, The British Cabinet gathered in the Lower House last night to discuss for two and a half hours. After 10:00 PM, the cabinet member of the Liberal Party, Samuel, came out of the meeting room and gave the government platform submitted to the election districts to the Liberal Party members to read. The discussion did not yield any results, so the Liberal Party members decided to continue the discussion today. The cabinet meeting did not end until 11:30 PM. Prime Minister McDonald is scheduled to give a speech to the public in Fine Hawn at 10:00 AM this morning. The cabinet will also gather today, but the Prime Minister will not be able to attend the meeting. Newspapers said that the chaotic and uncertain times are now over, and the people are willing to bear the pain of paying 2 million pounds for the election.

Reuters, London, 50,000 unemployed workers in Glasgow, Scotland, organized a demonstration against the measure stipulated in the National Government's austerity plan to reduce unemployment benefits. The mounted police had no choice but to use batons to attack the crowd, and many people were injured. The crowd attacked the police with broken bottles and other objects, so several policemen were also injured. Many glass windows were smashed by the crowd, and some shops were looted. Congress Party member McGovern and eleven others have been detained for inciting riots.

Reuters, London, After midnight in Glasgow, the riots broke out again, coupled with organized looting. Butter and other things were thrown all over the ground. When the police rushed to the scene, the crowd threw bottles and cans from the shops at them. Most of the glass windows in the shops were broken, and various items were scattered on the road. The mounted police charged several times, and order was restored at 2:00 AM.

Reuters, London, When the Lower House met this morning, the riots in Glasgow last night were mentioned. Left-wing Congress Party members expressed dissatisfaction with the Secretary of State for Scottish Affairs Sinclair's defense of the Glasgow police. Another left-wing member was even more激烈, disobeying the speaker's warning, stood up and shouted, "You can do whatever you want. We will fight against the legal authority. Either you take our lives, or we take yours."

Reuters, London, The National Government has proposed a bill to prohibit raising food prices during emergencies caused by the decline in the pound. The bill authorizes the Ministry of Commerce to prevent monopolizing food supplies or unreasonably raising prices without reason. Violators will be sentenced to three months in prison, a fine of one hundred pounds, and confiscation of goods. The first reading of this bill has been passed.

Reuters, London, The provisions of the financial bill, which contain the government's proposal to exchange bonds, have now been passed by the Lower House. British five-percent war bonds are a type of bond whose interest is not subject to income tax, so they are loved by foreigners and overseas British people. The government now plans to recover 200 million pounds of five-percent war bonds and replace them with new bonds with lower interest rates and shorter redemption periods, but it does not force the recovery, but only asks bondholders to accept this method.

French Prime Minister to Visit the United States

Scheduled to Depart on the 16th of This Month

Budget Deficit, Banks Closed

French Finance Also Showing Shakes

National Daily, Paris, French Prime Minister Laval's trip to the United States has now been decided. He will leave France on the 16th of this month and take the French ship France west. During Laval's departure from France, his duties will be taken over by the Minister of Justice, Peraire, and former Prime Minister Tateyo will be transferred to the Minister of the Interior, as the Interior is also a part-time job of Laval.

National Daily, Paris, French Prime Minister Laval claimed today that new taxes could be avoided in next year's budget. The total budget is about 500 million francs, and it is hoped that revenue and expenditure will offset each other. The budget is often the most controversial issue for the French government, and many cabinets have been overthrown because of this. According to Laval's budget for this year, the deficit is about 20 billion to 30 billion francs, so next year's government expenses must be reduced, but fortunately, taxes can still be avoided.

National Daily, Paris, The French Cοmtoir Lyon Allemand Bank suddenly closed its doors today and stopped cashing. The bank's capital is 210 million francs, but the bank has not yet reported the liquidation to the authorities, so it may be a temporary measure to avoid a run. However, the financial situation in France has already shown a shake.

Gandhi Plans to Tour Europe After the Round Table Conference Ends

Various Ethnic Groups Compete for Seats in Congress

It Is Definitely Not Something That Can Be Resolved in a Moment

National Daily, Berlin, After the end of the London Round Table Conference, it is heard that Gandhi will tour Europe. His itinerary will probably start from the British capital to Hamburg, Germany, to meet with the so-called "Believers in Nature," Chikomann. Chikomann will accompany Gandhi and others on a tour of Europe, because Chikomann and Gandhi are old friends in India. Because Chikomann walked around the world several years ago and became close friends with Gandhi after meeting him in India, Chikomann returned to Europe and devoted himself to the Indian independence movement and promoted a new religion in Europe. The teachings of this religion are quite similar to Taoism.

Reuters, London, Indian Hindus, Muslims, and other small ethnic groups are competing for seats in the Indian Round Table Conference, which is difficult to reconcile, so the Minority Committee will suspend the meeting for a week starting today in order to hold informal talks. Indian Hindu Gandhi and Muslim Aga Khan have discussed several times, but there is no solution.

Women in Spain Enjoy Suffrage

Reuters, Madrid, The Spanish Congress today debated the women's suffrage bill. A proposal that women must be over 45 years old to have the right to vote was ultimately rejected, and a proposal that women over 23 years old have the right to vote was passed by a vote of 170 to 121. Two female congressmen had different opinions on this proposal and debated fiercely. One opposed the proposal based on the theory that women's political education has not yet begun, and the other said that women have also contributed to the success of the Spanish Republic and should enjoy political rights.

Telegram from Beiping

To All Newspaper Offices: Japanese imperialists are intentionally annexing Manchuria and Mongolia to realize their continental policy. This has been planned for a long time. They have repeatedly used conspiracies against our Northeast, like a wild boar and a long snake, devouring our country. The Twenty-One Demands of the fourth year of the Republic of China, the Jinan Massacre of the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, and the recent cases of the Wan and Korean incidents are shameful and humiliating, accumulating for a long time and becoming more profound. Now, taking advantage of our internal unrest and the severe floods, when the people of the country are trying to save the dying and help the living, they openly send troops to the Eastern Provinces, attacking Liaoning and Jilin. Famous cities and important towns have been captured, with burning, killing, looting, and all kinds of inhumane atrocities. They gain an inch and advance a foot, and their ferocious flames are spreading endlessly. Important News: The Course of the Japanese Army's Capture of Changji

From the 19th to the 26th

Changchun Correspondence: The Japanese army heard that Shenyang was occupied on the night of the 18th, and began military operations in Changchun at 2:00 AM the next morning. They then advanced from Changchun to capture Jilin. The details of the continuous course of events are recorded as follows:

The Japanese Army's Attack on Changchun: At about 10:00 PM on September 18, the Japanese army began attacking Beidaying in Liaoning Province. At about 2:00 AM the next morning, the Changchun Japanese Army Brigade Headquarters received an order from the Kwantung Army Headquarters to mobilize and attack Changchun. They immediately dispatched teams to surround and attack the military camp of the Luguanzi Railway Army, which was guarding the station. Battalion Commander Fu Guanjun of the camp, thinking it was a normal field exercise, went out to investigate and was shot down by the Japanese army. They then began attacking the Eastern Railway Section 6 Police Station, which was adjacent to the camp, and the Eastern Province Special Zone Police Branch. Major Captain Qian of the Japanese army, with the mediation of Sun, the director of the Jilin Province Military and Police Inspection Office stationed there, ordered the troops of the office to surrender their weapons. Director Sun traveled back and forth between the Chinese and Japanese troops to mediate, and at the same time, he telegraphed Xi Qia, the chief of staff of the Jilin Border Defense Army Headquarters, by long-distance telephone for instructions. Xi replied that there was no need to resist. At this time, the soldiers of the camp had suffered many casualties, and because the battalion commander was shot and killed, they were extremely激昻 and refused to surrender their weapons. Some retreated northward. When the attack began, the sound of guns and cannons shook the city. After the army in the camp surrendered their weapons, the Railway Police and Special Zone Police there also surrendered their weapons together. The Japanese army immediately occupied the area and cut off the telephone lines connecting the area with other places. At about 6:00 AM on the same day, the brigade commander of the Japanese army stationed in Changchun led his troops to surround and attack the Nanling military camp, which was about three miles south of Changchun City. The garrison there had a artillery regiment, an infantry regiment, and a baggage battalion. The first to be attacked was the artillery regiment. The regiment headquarters telegraphed Xi Qia by long-distance telephone for instructions. Xi also replied, "Do not resist." The regimental and battalion officers there, because they could not resist and could not sit and wait for death, gradually retreated from each other, and the stored military equipment, food, and barracks were all burned by the Japanese army. The guns, cannons, and horses were also taken away. By about 8:00 PM on this day, the Japanese army began to return to Toudaogou, which was an annexed land of the South Manchuria Railway.

The Japanese Army's Advance from Changchun to Jilin: From the morning of the 19th, after the Japanese army occupied Kuanchengzi Station, the telegraph and telephone lines between Changchun and Harbin were all cut off. At about 8:00 PM on the same day, the important parts of the radio station were dismantled and Japanese soldiers were sent to guard them. On the morning of the 20th, the telegraph bureau of the city was also sealed off, and the long-distance telephone lines of the telegraph bureau were cut off. Only telephone calls within the city were allowed, and Japanese soldiers were sent to guard them separately. The intention was to cut off the connection between Jilin and Changchun. At the same time, armored vehicles also drove to Changchun from the south, and the Japanese military department retrieved the timetable for the Jilin-Changchun train. Japanese nationals in Jilin also came to Changchun one after another. The symbol of their advance to Jilin has been clearly revealed. Xi Qia learned of the above situation on the evening of the 20th and sent Diplomatic Director Shi Luben to question Shizhu Taigoro, the Japanese consul in Jilin. The reply was that there was

The Entire City's Labor Sector Held a Representative Assembly Yesterday

Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, the city's labor sector held a representative assembly at the City Party Headquarters to discuss the issue of resisting Japan and saving the nation. They issued a letter to workers of the world and sent telegrams to the central government and the Guangdong faction, requesting unity against external enemies. They also resolved to request the city government to punish the perpetrators of the shooting of unarmed civilians by the Fifth District Public Security Bureau on Zhabei Baoshan Road with the most severe penalties. Details are recorded below:

Attending Organizations: Yesterday's attendees included over 150 labor unions from various industries such as postal services and publishing, leather manufacturing, hat making, bookbinding, Western cuisine, letterpress printing, silk reeling, tea manufacturing, military uniforms, laundry, dyeing, soap and medicine, toothbrush manufacturing, pharmaceutical industry, traditional Chinese medicine, sauce making, journalism, newspaper distribution, incense making, tea and snack shops, lithography, silk reeling in districts 3, 4, and 6, knitting in districts 1, 2, and 6, cigarette rolling in districts 3, 4, 5, and 6, water and electricity in districts 1, 2, and 6, cotton spinning in districts 3, 4, 5, and 10, dockworkers, inland river shipping, and public transportation. There were over 500 representatives, including Hou Dachun, Lu Jingshi, Yang Youren, Chen Peide, and Zhu Xuefan.

Meeting Proceedings: (1) Everyone stood at attention; (2) Paid the highest respects to the Party and National Flag and Sun Yat-sen's portrait; (3) Read Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will; (4) Observed three minutes of silence; (5) The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting; (6) Representatives who petitioned in Nanjing reported; (7) Representatives from higher authorities gave guidance; (8) Discussion; (9) Speeches; (10) Slogans; (11) Adjournment. The presidium consisted of five people: Hou Dachun, Lu Jingshi, Wang Wenhua, Chen Peide, and Fu Dewei. The master of ceremonies was Yue Yaqing, and the recorder was Guo Jiguang.

Chairman's Report: Fu Dewei reported on behalf of the presidium, stating that the significance of convening this representative assembly today is that after the invasion and occupation of the Northeast by the violent Japanese, the entire city's labor sector should urge the government to express resolute and effective countermeasures. At this critical moment of national crisis, we should thoroughly sever economic ties with Japan and unite as a whole to serve as a strong backing for the government. We should awaken workers around the world to the violent acts of Japan in destroying world peace and express sympathy for us and provide us with practical assistance, and so on.

Report on the Petition: Representatives who petitioned in Nanjing, Zhang Kechang, Miao Hongjun, and Lu Muqin, reported that after arriving in Nanjing, the central government sent Ding Weifen, Zhang Daofan, and Fang Juehui to meet them. They gave detailed replies to our nine requests. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek also sent Chen Lifu as a representative to meet them and expressed great comfort regarding the labor representatives' petitions. Later, they went to see Mr. Hu Hanmin and had a conversation for about an hour. He expressed that he was willing to do his best to serve the Party and the country. After the report was completed, Mr. Zhu Maocheng gave a speech.

(2) The assembly will send a telegram to the central government and the National Government requesting them to immediately send troops to resist Japan. Resolved and passed. (3) The assembly will send a telegram to comrades Hu Hanmin and Wang Jingwei, requesting them to immediately take on difficult tasks. Resolved and passed. (4) A telegram will be sent to workers nationwide, urging them to unanimously and absolutely sever economic ties with Japan. Resolved and passed. (5) A telegram will be sent to the central government requesting them to promptly order relief for Chinese workers in Japanese factories. Resolved and passed. (6) A telegram will be sent to workers nationwide, urging them to unanimously and closely organize volunteer armies as a backing for the government and requesting the central government to provide military equipment. Resolved and passed. (7) Severe punishment of treacherous merchants and all treacherous people. Resolved and suggested that the Anti-Japanese Association handle it strictly. (8) Request the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to order all factories, merchants, and shops in the city to hand over all existing Japanese goods to the Anti-Japanese Association for safekeeping within ten days. Starting from October 11th, inspections will be carried out. If any shops or factories are found to have Japanese goods, they will be charged as treacherous merchants. Resolved and passed. Resolved and passed. On the night of September 18th, the Japanese troops stationed in the three northeastern provinces suddenly attacked Shenyang, Changchun, Yingkou, Andong, and other places without warning, and occupied them completely without resistance. They then began a chaotic massacre of defenseless civilians, regardless of gender or age, raping women, burning cities, and destroying everything. A unit of troops forcibly occupied the Shenyang Arsenal. The Chinese soldiers did not resist, but when they entered, they injured about 30 to 35 workers inside with hand grenades and bayonets. Furthermore, Japan falsely claims to have special rights in the three northeastern provinces, but in reality, it does not have any special rights. Japan's special rights in the three northeastern provinces and the right to station troops along the South Manchurian Railway are based on the demands of the Twenty-One Demands in 1915, but those demands have never been approved by China's legislative bodies, so they are naturally invalid. We Chinese workers vow with the utmost sincerity to save the Chinese nation and all of humanity from the trampling of Japanese imperialism and militarism. Fellow workers, rise up and fight with us!

Resolved to Establish a Disciplinary Committee

Second Declaration of the Journalism Labor Union

To all oppressed people of China: Japanese imperialism has occupied our three northeastern provinces by force, massacred thousands of civilians, destroyed the entire social foundation of the north, deprived us of our national sovereignty and seized our rights. The terrible news has been spreading for nearly half a month. In these two weeks, the problem has not only not been solved at all, but the situation in all aspects has made it very clear and certain that the only way to solve the problem is for our people across the country to unite and fight Japanese imperialists to the death. Japanese imperialists are still actively attacking us, and the crisis of national subjugation is imminent. How is Japanese imperialism invading us, and how did it pre-arrange our three northeastern provinces? This is a question worthy of our great attention, and as long as we carefully review the situation before and after the incident, we can understand. For more than ten years, who doesn't know that the three northeastern provinces are a den of pro-Japanese warlords and bureaucrats. Although those pro-Japanese warlords and bureaucrats are Chinese on the surface, officials of China, and subordinates under the rule of the Chinese government, in reality, they are all lackeys of Japan, filial sons and grandsons of Japan. Therefore, for more than ten years, the three northeastern provinces have only been considered Chinese territory in name, but in essence, they have long become Japanese colonies. All political and economic power in the three northeastern provinces is entirely in the hands of the Japanese. However, the greedy and insatiable Japanese still feel that it is not enough, and they must thoroughly plunder the land and make it their formal territory in order to be happy. This dispatch of troops is the beginning of plunder. However, clever and cunning Japanese, in order to deceive the public, will force several Chinese traitors to organize an independent country after directly dispatching troops, blatantly seceding from China and throwing themselves into the arms of the Japanese. This is the old method of dealing with Korea, so our three northeastern provinces will become the second Korea. The people of the three provinces will soon become slaves of a conquered nation. Now, news from all sides is confirming the possibility and reliability of this fact, so what else is there to question? Alas, our China is still in a state of confusion and unconsciousness at this most critical moment, and it wants peace, non-resistance, and seeks the help of the League of Nations. What is this? Alas, the omen of national subjugation! Peace, peace, who doesn't like this word? However, the peace that is sought in this way is the peace of national subjugation, the peace of extinction, not the peace that is beneficial to the people. China's peace has long been destroyed by itself for decades, so what peace is there to speak of? Our people take out so much of their blood and sweat every year to support officials and troops, but as a result, when foreign aggression comes, they don't know to rise up and resist, but just weakly beg for forgiveness from the robbers and tell their own people to want peace and should not resist, and give up thousands of miles of territory to the dwarves in peace. Thinking about it, it is so painful! As for the League of Nations, it is even more unreliable. What is the League of Nations? To put it plainly, the League of Nations is an organization of imperialists united to oppress weak nations. The League of Nations oppresses weak nations, and is the executioner of weak nations. Where can it stand up for justice for us? The facts of the past few days have told us that it not only does not interfere with Japan's violence, but is tacitly allowing Japan to continue its violence and carve up the three northeastern provinces. Once the three northeastern provinces formally become Japanese territory, they will follow up and attack China, and divide China from the standpoint of "equal benefits." Therefore, the League of Nations is definitely not our savior, but our enemy! However, there are still many Chinese with noble words who are fantasizing about the help of the League of Nations, which is really shameful and ridiculous. The enemy has already raised the butcher knife and is chasing us closely. We don't know to escape, don't know to resist, just pray to the gods and worship Buddha, and make those unpromising stupid acts. How painful it is! Now the situation in all aspects is so dangerous and urgent. If we want to save China, save ourselves, and not be slaves of a conquered nation, we can only rely on our own courage to automatically unite and fight against enemies at home and abroad. Now, at this critical juncture of national subjugation and extinction, there is no second way to survive except self-rescue. Japan will not be merciful, will not wake up, will not "lay down the butcher knife and become a Buddha on the spot." The League of Nations will not uphold justice and help us. The government is so weak and traitorous, and in this state, only we, the people, can rise up and fight Japan without compromise. Peace has long ceased to exist, and non-resistance is a good way to destroy the country. Tranquility is just equal to being calmly slaughtered by Japanese imperialists. Compatriots who are unwilling to be slaves of a conquered nation, rise up, bravely, thoroughly, and without compromise: (1) Automatically arm yourselves and declare war on Japan; (2) Drive Japanese troops out of the country; (3) Do not work with Japanese people, do not provide Japanese residents with food and all items; (4) Mercilessly kill treacherous merchants who collude with Japanese people; (5) Recover all privileges of Japanese imperialism in China; (6) Confiscate all property of Japanese imperialists in China as compensation for the losses in the three northeastern provinces; (7) Oppose all internal disputes and unite against foreign enemies; (8) Oppose the policy of non-resistance and tranquility that will destroy the country; (9) Oppose secret diplomacy and the signing of treaties that cede rights and humiliate the country; (10) Down with imperialism; (11) Abolish all unequal treaties.

May the People of the Country Pay Attention to the Area of the Three Northeastern Provinces

Greater Than the Seven Coastal Provinces

According to a geographer yesterday, the total area of the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang is 3,533,000 square miles, which is larger than the seven coastal provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, and Guangxi. The total area of the seven provinces is only 3,447,500 square miles, which is 84,700 square miles less in comparison. Therefore, the people of the country should quickly wake up and understand that not an inch of national territory can be lost, let alone the great Northeastern Provinces.

Yesterday Entertained the Movie and Education Sectors

Page 14

Negotiated Anti-Japanese Propaganda Methods

According to the National News Agency, the propaganda department of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, on the afternoon of the first (1st) at 5 PM, entertained local newspaper reporters at the Ningbo Fellow Association to discuss propaganda methods. Yesterday (10th) at 10 AM and 1 PM, it convened a joint meeting of local cinemas' propaganda and a joint meeting of anti-Japanese national salvation associations of major secondary schools on the third floor of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Request each representative to be responsible for assisting the anti-Japanese national salvation association of each school in carrying out national salvation work. Another representative suggested that we should have a definite goal in opposing Japan. Then the representative of Meizhuan said that we do not need to put forward any anti-Japanese goals. What we need at present is how to oppose Japan and how to promote it to awaken the people of the country, which is the most important task, and so on.

A Mass Meeting Held in Zhuanqiao Town

Five Thousand Farmers, Merchants, and Students Attended

The Anti-Japanese Movement Propaganda Week held by the Shanghai County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association yesterday was rotated to the Third District. The chairman reported that the Anti-Japanese Association has two requests for all compatriots today: one is to sever diplomatic relations with Japan, and the other is to prepare to declare war on Japan, because only these two paths can save China and put Japanese imperialism to death. The chairman finished the report, shouted slogans at the end, and the meeting adjourned at dusk.

Proposals Passed: (1) Sending a telegram to the central government requesting severance of diplomatic relations with Japan; (2) Sending a telegram to the central government requesting the dispatch of troops to declare war on Japan on a specific date; (3) Sending a telegram to the central government requesting the Ministry of Education to order all schools above middle school level nationwide to strictly implement military training; (4) Sending a telegram to the central government requesting the appointment of Chiang Kai-shek as the commander-in-chief to fight Japan; (5) Sending a telegram to the central government requesting Chiang Kai-shek to preside over military affairs, Wang Jingwei to preside over party affairs, and Hu Hanmin to preside over political affairs; (6) Petitioning the central government to promptly order the Ministry of Industry to raise funds to establish state-owned factories to accommodate Chinese workers in Japanese factories and thoroughly implement economic severance with Japan.

Because the violent Japanese are invading more and more urgently, and the country's demise is imminent, it is necessary to gather the elites of the whole country to jointly plan the major affairs of the party and the country. In the past, only personal political differences caused fragmentation, and now the trend of public opinion and the repeated declarations of the country by all of you also said that unity and resistance to foreign aggression are necessary. Therefore, we urge you to immediately abandon past grievances, gather together, and each display your abilities to manage the party, government, and military in order to save China from danger and resist foreign aggression, and then achieve world harmony and eliminate obstacles. Quick Mail Telegram from the Fifth Division Party Headquarters.

All newspapers are requested to forward this to all compatriots across the country: Japanese capitalist imperialists, in order to reliably and abundantly supply all raw materials to prepare for the impending Second World War, and to save their incurable economic panic that has lasted for several years to maintain their domestic politics that are on the verge of collapse, decided to make their Manchuria-Mongolia policy, which they have been planning since the Meiji era, suddenly become white-hot, betray the non-war pact, break international precedents, and blatantly, under various pretexts, use extremely rapid and brutal means to send troops to occupy our three northeastern provinces. After the incident, they even fabricated facts, covered up the truth, rejected the mediation of the League of Nations, and continued to increase troops to successively occupy famous cities, attempting to permanently occupy the eastern provinces. It is because Japanese imperialism has now decisively re-enacted the scene of robbing Korea. Our compatriots across the country, facing this serious invasion, must not rely solely on the assistance that cannot be obtained by third parties, but can only hope to survive. Only by exerting all our own strength, uniting as one, and meeting head-on can we open up a path to survival. And the development of this path to survival cannot be accomplished without sweeping away all Japanese forces in China. All armed comrades of this division, filled with grief and indignation, are waiting with swords and pillows to take the lead for the country and stand on the front line to fight the Japanese bandits to the death. We earnestly hope that our compatriots across the country will rise up in time, closely organize and strengthen their forces, make long-term plans, and prepare to go to the national crisis with a determination to die. The survival of the country depends on this one action. We are willing to make the final great determination together. Executive Committee of the Special Party Department of the Fifth Division of the Army, under seal. News from Shipping in the Anti-Japanese Voice.

Students Studying in Japan and Others Are Returning Home One After Another

Students Studying in Japan Return Home: After the violent Japanese forcibly occupied our eastern provinces, students studying in Japan felt the pain of the loss of national territory and were particularly embarrassed to be within the sphere of influence of the violent Japanese. Therefore, a part of the students have returned home from Japan, and those who have returned to Shanghai from Japan in recent days include Wang Qiyuan, Zhang Weijin, Li Yuanchao, Lin Yihui, Huang Zhengcheng, Zheng Jingwei, Tang Zhenmin, Fu Tongde, Yuan Yaqun, Zhang Jianren, Xie Shijian, Chen Weiyi, Cai Qiuwu, and dozens of others. A large number of students are still waiting for travel expenses, and will set off to return home after the money is remitted.

Overseas Chinese Return Home After Being Insulted: Most of the overseas Chinese in Japan are engaged in hairdressing, kimono, and cooking. Since the Japanese soldiers occupied Liaoning and Jilin on the 19th of last month, they have suffered various insults. Therefore, the overseas Chinese have left Japan and returned home one after another. The Ikoma Maru arrived in Shanghai yesterday, carrying 129 people including Fu Zhenghua. The Kasagi Maru arrived in Shanghai, and there were another 43 people including Xie Wenhua and Gu Qiyun. The Rokko Maru and Mikasa Maru arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, with a total of more than 210 people including Chen Qianyuan, Chen Huajun, and Bao Dequan, mostly from Zhejiang and Fujian provinces. A large number of overseas Chinese will also arrive in Shanghai within two or three days.

Li Zifang Has Resigned: Li Zifang, the Chinese manager of Nippon Yusen Kaisha, submitted his resignation to Nippon Yusen after receiving the notice from the Anti-Japanese Association, which has been approved. Starting yesterday, he has been liquidating the accounts of the comprador's department, and will leave the relationship after settlement. Other Chinese employees are also willing to resign unanimously. Zhang Xueliang's Telegram Reply to the Letter from the Taiwanese Remnants.

Preparations for Beijing-Guangdong Peace Negotiations Move to Shanghai for Resumption

Chiang Kai-shek Orders Chen Mingshu and Others Back to Nanjing

Guangdong Faction Sends Official Representatives to Shanghai

(Hong Kong) The Nanjing-Guangdong peace talks resumed at 3 p.m. on the 1st. The Guangdong side presented six concrete conditions. The Nanjing representatives found them satisfactory but still needed to telegraph Chiang Kai-shek for instructions. The clause regarding the release of Hu Hanmin and Li Jishen was changed to "inviting Hu and others to Shanghai to participate in a unified conference." Chen Mingshu received a reply telegram from Chiang yesterday, ordering Chen and others to return to Nanjing immediately. Therefore, the peace conference will be moved to Shanghai. Chiang's telegram did not mention any intention to step down. Discussions will continue at 3 p.m. on the 2nd. The Guangdong National Government decided at its meeting on the 2nd to send official representatives to Shanghai to participate in the peace talks. The number of representatives is set at three. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Hong Kong) News from the Guangdong National Government: Many telegrams calling for peace have been received here. A peace agreement is expected to be negotiated within five days. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Hong Kong) Cai Yuanpei and Zhang Ji visited Zhu Zhaoxin on the 2nd to discuss Northeast diplomacy. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Hong Kong) Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce representative Wang Hanliang and others petitioned the Guangdong National Government for a cessation of hostilities and a united front against external threats on the 1st. They were received by Tang Shaoyi, Wang Jingwei, and Gu Yingfen, and the outcome was satisfactory. Wang and others returned to Shanghai on the 2nd. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) Regarding the Beijing-Guangdong peace issue, the six points reported by the Hong Kong telegram were described here as Cai Yuanpei's telegrams, which did not list conditions. Military and financial matters are particularly intertwined. Regarding the selection of the Minister of Finance, at least the consent of the highest military officer is required. Furthermore, the party operates on a collegial system, and it cannot be said that it should be handed over to someone to preside over. As for administrative issues, those willing to step aside are doing so. Moreover, Hu Hanmin has been able to receive guests freely starting today. He also stated that Wang Zhengting's mishandling of diplomacy was wrong, and the public opposition was justified. As for the unified conference, the name is still under consideration and has not been definitively decided, but the location is in Shanghai, and both Beijing and Guangdong have fully agreed. Tang Shaoyi and others will travel to Shanghai soon. Liu Luyin, representing Guangzhou, arrived in Shanghai yesterday. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Nanjing) Yesterday, representatives from the Shanghai labor community visited Hu Hanmin, requesting him to return to his duties. Hu stated that he would speak frankly and without reservation about the major plans for the party and the nation. Now that the nation is facing difficulties, the people should pay attention to revitalizing politics, developing the economy, and seeking national unity, and confront Japan with a unified national force. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Lindbergh and His Wife Encountered Danger in Airplane in Hankou

All Three Fell into the Water but Were Rescued

(Hankou) This morning, Mr. and Mrs. Lindbergh planned to accompany Jin, a medical officer from the National Government's Health Department, in an airplane to survey Dongting Lake. The plane was unloaded from the British aircraft carrier HMS Hermes onto the water. Lindbergh himself was piloting the plane. As the plane took off, one wing suddenly tilted downward, and the plane flipped over in an instant. All three fell into the water. Lindbergh helped his wife with all his strength. A lifeboat from HMS Hermes happened to be on the ship's side and rushed to rescue the three, taking them aboard HMS Hermes. Fortunately, all three were unharmed. Although Mrs. Lindbergh was frightened, she remained calm. The overturned plane was then towed onto HMS Hermes. Upon inspection, it was found that one wing and other parts were damaged, but they could not be repaired in Hankou. It was decided that HMS Hermes would carry the plane to Shanghai for repairs on Saturday evening. Mr. and Mrs. Lindbergh will also travel east on the same ship. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

Roads in Hankou Awaiting Repair

(Hankou) Fang Benren stated that the recent relief efforts will focus on repairing the roads in Hankou, which will be handled by a committee formed by the branch association. Currently, Wang Shiliu and others are planning the project. The general association has already received 800,000 yuan, which will be used to purchase clothing and provide food, as well as to plan the construction of low-income housing to solve the immediate problems of the disaster victims. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Hankou) Li Jin has arrived in Nanchang and will return to Hankou in the coming days. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

(Hankou) The disaster relief meeting decided to form a committee to repair the roads in Hankou, providing work as relief. Wang Shiliu and others were appointed as committee members. The emergency relief meeting decided to build 10,000 temporary shelters in Hankou. (Special dispatch, 2nd)

Xiaoshan

Methods for Inspecting Japanese Goods: The Xiaoshan National Salvation and Anti-Japanese Association has stipulated that all kinds of Japanese goods must be sold out within ten days and never imported again. Various unsold Japanese goods will be inspected and registered by the inspection team, then either sealed or sold off. A list must be compiled and displayed within one month. If any private import of Japanese goods occurs again, strict punishment will be imposed upon discovery. The County Chamber of Commerce has telegraphed the provincial government and the Provincial Executive Committee to file a record.

Organizing Voluntary Defense Corps in All Townships: The Xiaoshan County Government received an order from the provincial government yesterday, forwarding it to all districts and townships to expedite the establishment of voluntary defense corps. At a time when the nation is facing internal and external troubles, the people should seek self-defense. All those aged between twenty and forty are required to undergo training. All townships must establish corps within one month. One platoon leader will be selected for every five hundred households and sent to the county government for training. They will then return to their villages to serve as instructors, training the people to organize voluntary defense corps.

Hefei

Changlinhe Town Entirely Robbed: Changlinhe, a major town in the southeast along Chaohu Lake, is a fish-producing area with thriving commerce. Lake bandits have long coveted it, but they have been unable to invade because the town's merchants' corps and water and land police have maintained strict defenses. However, on the morning of the 25th, due to the Mid-Autumn Festival, the city was crowded, and the corps police were busy with the holiday, with lax defenses. Suddenly, fourteen large boats, fully loaded with two or three hundred water bandits, swarmed ashore, surrounded the town, and stormed in through the north and south gates. The garrisoned corps police were caught off guard and retreated under the leadership of Corps Commander Gong Ruiting. The bandits then arbitrarily searched and robbed every household along the streets. Hundreds of large and small businesses in the town were spared. Before leaving, they also kidnapped sixty or seventy wealthy merchants and fled to the center of the lake. The losses are estimated at over 100,000 yuan. The businesses of Liu Renhe and Yude Tai, among others, suffered the greatest losses. Today (the 26th), people from the town flocked to the city to report the case. The county government urgently dispatched a large detachment of self-defense corps to pursue and suppress the bandits. Furthermore, Sanhe Town, a famous rice-producing area ninety li south, is also currently under siege by several hundred bandits. On the 25th, the new County Magistrate Zhu Tingliao, along with the Self-Defense Corps Commander Yuan Doushu, led a team to suppress them.

Educational News Highlights

How Should the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Principals' Conference

Lead Students to Save the Nation?

Ten Measures Decided

(Zhenjiang Correspondence) The principals of Jiangsu provincial middle schools gathered in Zhenjiang Middle School on September 30th. Over ten people attended, including Principal Hu from Suzhou Middle School, Principal Zheng from Shanghai Middle School, Principal Gu from Taizhou Middle School, Principal Zhang from Nantong Middle School, Principal Zhou from Yangzhou Middle School, Principal Ren from Zhenjiang Middle School, Principal Chen from Suzhou Women's Middle School, and Principal Jiang from Songjiang Women's Middle School. They resolved nine proposals, the most important being two: (1) How to lead students to overcome national difficulties together. Ten measures were decided: (1) Teachers and students of each school should jointly form an anti-Japanese national salvation association to actively work; (2) Each subject should temporarily incorporate anti-Japanese national salvation teaching materials within a possible scope to meet the current extraordinary needs; (3) Teachers and students in various primary and secondary schools should jointly swear to always use pure domestic products and economically sever ties with Japan, extending from teachers and students themselves to their families and then gradually to society; (4) All faculty and staff of each school should wear domestic-made uniforms from now on to boost morale; (5) Principals Hu and Zheng should be nominated as representatives to request the Directorate-General of Military Training to issue militia forces to each school, with usable guns and ammunition for practice; (6) Each school should request the local garrison to send military officers to the school to assist in training, or lead militia schools to the garrison's camp to temporarily borrow guns for practice; (7) All girls' schools should increase nursing courses and organize nursing teams; (8) A letter should be sent to the Directorate-General of Military Training requesting that military instructors with excellent performance in each school not be transferred to other positions in order to deepen their training (9) Each school should pay close attention to this series of national salvation work, striving to achieve practical and lasting results, and avoid temporary extravagance and recklessness, or allowing enthusiasm to wane after the situation has passed (10) A telegram should be sent to the National Government to quickly decide on a strategy for armed self-defense and to the Guangdong side to jointly resist foreign aggression in order to alleviate the national crisis (2) How to promote donations for disaster relief. Three items were resolved: (1) Upon investigation, primary school teachers in various disaster areas are also affected by disasters, but because they are civil servants, they often cannot receive relief. This is extremely difficult, and the Department of Education should be urgently requested to allocate all the funds deducted from the salaries of faculty and staff of each school to specifically provide relief to primary school teachers affected by disasters. At the same time, contact public and private universities to do the same. As for the method of providing on-site relief, the Department of Education should convene the heads of education bureaus and the principals of each school in each county to coordinate it. (2) In addition to the stipulated salary deduction to help relief efforts, each school will raise more donations to provide emergency relief, the more the better. (3) The total amount of donations from each school must be reported for comparison and summarized and announced.

Eighth Meeting of the University Students' Executive Committee

Representative Assembly to Be Held This Sunday Afternoon

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of students from various universities in the city held its eighth meeting of the executive committee yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m. in the conference room of the Xiaonanmen Youth Propaganda Group to discuss the progress of all association affairs. Details of the meeting are recorded below:

Executive committee members present: Cao Shuyi from Tongwen Chinese Department, Li Yuansu from Daxia University, Zhu Youhuan from Guanghua University, Li Chunsun from the Faculty of Law and Politics, Gu Shiyu from Datong University, Zhang Shousong from Shanghai Law School, Liu Xuantian from Jiaotong University, and Peng Qixin from Fudan University.

Meeting Details: The chairman was Liu Xuantian, the standing executive committee member, and the recorder was Li Chunsun, the document section executive committee member. After the formalities were completed, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting and then proceeded to the discussion.

Resolutions: (1) The case of Chinese students from Tongwen College transferring schools: Resolved to hand it over to the standing committee to contact the Municipal Government Education Bureau to exempt them from the qualification examination and, if necessary, to request the Ministry of Education to handle it by telegram. (2) Whether the date of the executive committee's regular meeting should be changed: Resolved to hold meetings twice a week, to be ratified by the representative assembly, with the dates set for Tuesday and Saturday afternoons from 4:00 p.m. to 6:00 p.m. (3) Whether the office hours of the executive committee should be changed after the resumption of classes: Resolved to set them for 4:00 p.m. to 6:00 p.m. daily. (4) The case of the association hiring a clerk: Resolved to hire a clerk, providing a monthly salary of 35 yuan, to be handled by the document section. (5) The case of filming the Japanese atrocities: Resolved to hand it over to the propaganda section. (6) The case of the strike by workers at the Japanese cotton mill: Resolved that the municipal party headquarters should be urged to handle it immediately, with representatives from the Faculty of Law and Politics and Daxia University going to the municipal party headquarters to make contact. (7) The case of the Baolu tragedy in Shanghai: Resolved that the association should petition the municipal party headquarters and the municipal government to severely punish the perpetrators and request guarantees that similar cases will not occur again in the future. (8) The case of the association's financial difficulties and a request to the municipal party headquarters to increase subsidies: Resolved that the document section should prepare a budget and request the municipal party headquarters to increase subsidies. (9) Questions regarding membership fees for each school: Resolved to be decided at the next representative assembly. (10) The time and location of the next representative meeting: Resolved to be held at 2:00 p.m. this Sunday afternoon at the Youth Propaganda Group. (11) To telegraph US President Hoover to expose the atrocities of Japanese soldiers in our eastern provinces and request him to uphold justice: Resolved that this proposal be temporarily reserved.

Two Instructions: The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association of Shanghai University Students issues Instruction No. 8 regarding instructions: In accordance with the resolution of the association's fourth representative assembly, classes will be resumed in each school from today (no later than next Monday) without further delay, and military training, propaganda work, and research on Sino-Japanese issues will be intensified. As for the detailed rules, they will be handled by each school according to the circumstances. You are hereby ordered to comply.

Interport Tennis

Opening Ceremony at 11:00 a.m.

丨Chinese Players Dominate, Schedule Tight丨

The fifth Shanghai-Hong Kong interport tennis tournament is scheduled to open today at 11:00 a.m. It will last for three days and be held at the French Chamber of Commerce lawn tennis grounds on Avenue Joffre. The opening match will be women's doubles. The schedule for today and tomorrow is extremely tight. Chinese players have a strong advantage. Malayan Overseas Chinese Tennis Team Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Four Track and Field Athletes Came Together

Female Athletes Temporarily Stayed in Hong Kong to Transfer to Guangdong

丨Led Back to Their Motherland by Wu Zaixing, Wang Shengzhi, etc.丨

For the purpose of promoting sports in various places in British Malaya, the All-Malaya Sports Games were held in April this year. Before the games, each port, such as Penang, Malacca, Kuala Lumpur, Seremban, Muar, Johor, Singapore, and Ipoh, first held its local joint sports meeting and then sent athletes to the games to participate. After the closing of the games, the athletes were selected and an overseas Chinese team was organized to represent Malaya in the National Games. Unfortunately, the National Games were postponed.

A Portion of the Malayan Overseas Chinese Track and Field Athletes (Photo by This Newspaper) (From left to right) He Yishi, Pan Nanshun, Liang Chonghua, Bo Baocheng, Wu Zaixing (Leader)

The Malayan Tennis Team (Photo by This Newspaper)

(From left to right) Wang Shengzhi (Secretary), Zhong Zhilin, Yang Lunzhang, Lin Wangsu, Feng Jiekun

The athletes, originally more than 70 people, were recalled midway in Hong Kong. However, the track and field athletes and Lin Wangsu, the all-Malaya tennis champion, and others, were very interested in visiting the motherland. Therefore, Wu Zaixing, a prominent figure in the sports world, and Wang Shengzhi, the secretary of the team, were responsible for leading the team. They took the Ardu to Shanghai from Hong Kong. More than 20 female athletes originally came on the same boat but changed their plans temporarily. The plan to stay in Hong Kong to transfer to Guangdong for competition and visit Shanghai was abandoned. Yesterday, Yang Yufen, secretary of Jinan University, Chen Zhang'e, director of physical education, and student representative Hao Chunde, and others went to the pier to welcome them. Qiu Feihai, a national tennis player, was also among those welcoming them and planned to shake hands with his old friend Lin Wangsu, but he could not wait long and left the pier first. The ship arrived at exactly 2:00 p.m., and passengers did not disembark until 4:00 p.m. This two-hour wait was relieved by meeting Lin Aimin, an overseas Chinese from Singapore, who talked about the state of sports among overseas Chinese. Mr. Lin was originally taking care of the athletes returning home, but the National Games were suspended due to an incident, and the enthusiasm of the overseas Chinese could only be given to the East River. This time, there are a total of ten overseas Chinese athletes, leaders, and secretaries who plan to stay temporarily at Jinan University and then travel to West Lake, Nanjing, Suzhou, and Beijing. Lin Wangsu and others in Shanghai may participate in disaster relief matches at the invitation of the Association for the Advancement of Cooperation. The four track and field athletes who have arrived will be joined by Deng Yuehan and Cai Wenli, who will come to Shanghai on the 6th along with the soccer team, and then play friendly matches against various universities in Shanghai. The names and achievements of the various staff and athletes who came to Shanghai are introduced below:

Wu Zaixing, leader, is the director of the Regulations Section of the Organizing Committee of the Association and has made great contributions to the Association. Mr. Wu is proficient in basketball and good at sprinting. He represented China at the 8th Far Eastern Games in 1927. He graduated from the Department of Economics of Xiamen University in Fujian. This time, he plans to enter the graduate school of Tsinghua University in Beijing to specialize in economics.

Wang Shengzhi, graduated from the Department of Political Science of Peking University (now renamed Beiping University), is the director of the Secretariat Section of the Organizing Committee and the reporter of the Malaysian-Chinese Sports Games. He is fluent in Chinese and skilled in communication. He is a versatile talent among overseas Chinese.

Lin Wangsu won the title of All-Malaya Tennis Champion in 1931.

Yang Lunzhang is the runner-up in this year's All-Malaya Tennis Championship and also won the Johor International Tennis Championship this year, winning glory for the Chinese community in the area.

Zhong Zhilin is the central figure among the full backs of the All-Malaya football team and is also proficient in tennis.

Feng Jiekun is young and ambitious and has a lively physique. He is a rising tennis star and made a shocking performance in Annam last year, making him a formidable new force.

Fu Jinsheng, nicknamed "Flying General," set a new record of 10 seconds in the 100-yard dash at the All-Malaya World Games in August and finished second in the 220-yard dash by a hair, with a time of 22.1 seconds, which can also be said to be amazing.

Deng Yuehan is a mainstay of the team, good at hurdles and skilled in jumping. He won the All-Malaya Individual Championship in April this year (arriving in Shanghai on the 6th).

Liang Junhua specializes in hurdles with a score of under 17 seconds and is also good at sprinting and long jump.

Pan Nanshun is a triathlon expert who won the first place in javelin and shot put at the National Games last year.

He Yishi is good at long-distance running and is a rising star.

Malayan Football Team

One Win and One Loss in Hong Kong

Lost the First Game 1-4

Won the Second Game 3-1

(Hong Kong Correspondent) The Malayan Overseas Chinese Football Team returned to China. It was originally planned to participate in the National Games and stop by Hong Kong to play interport matches. The team played twice in Hong Kong. The first time, the Hong Kong China Team won, with a score of 4-1. The second time, the Malayan Team won, with a score of 3-1. Hong Kong has a very good impression of the Malayan team's skills. The team is scheduled to come to Shanghai on the 6th and stay at the new Chinese YMCA premises in the French Concession. It is expected that when they meet the Shanghai China Team in the future, there will be an unprecedented and fierce battle.

Local News

Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement Heard Yesterday

Workers Throughout the City Telegraph the Central Government to Send Troops

Patriotic Chinese Resign from Japanese Businesses

Students Studying in Japan and Overseas Chinese Return to China One After Another

Continued Records

Baoshan Road Tragedy

Party, Military, and Government Joint Investigation Underway

Public Organizations Request Punishment for You Bolu

Wang Zhijing Succeeds as Fifth District Chief

Chen Xizeng Voluntarily Requests Punishment Yesterday

The Fifth District Public Security Bureau police of Zhabei Baoshan Road had a misunderstanding with the public the night before last. Police officers opened fire, killing two civilians and seriously injuring five. The details were recorded in yesterday's newspaper. What this newspaper heard yesterday is compiled and narrated below:

Zhang Qun's Remarks: Regarding the incident of Fifth District Public Security Bureau police officers shooting civilians for stopping soldiers from posting slogans at a sentry post, a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency went to the municipal government yesterday to visit Mayor Zhang Qun and inquire about the truth of the matter and subsequent measures. I was honored to receive a detailed reply, as follows. According to the conversation, the truth of the incident can be divided into two points. The first point was that a dispute arose between soldiers posting slogans and police officers, which attracted the attention of the public. However, after the district chief explained, the matter was resolved. However, the audience gathered more and more, and then the second problem arose. After the matter of posting slogans was resolved, although the crowd gradually dispersed, some busybodies still inquired about the truth from the residents on the left and right. That morning, a Japanese merchant went to the Fifth District Public Security Bureau to negotiate the return of wheat bran detained by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association on Suzhou Creek Road. The Japanese had negotiated this matter several times, but it had not been returned. Therefore, those in the surrounding shops who witnessed the Japanese entering and leaving told the crowd and speculated, mistakenly believing that the Fifth District's ban on posting slogans was colluding with the Japanese. At this critical moment of national crisis, patriotic actions are naturally shared by everyone. Therefore, the general public gathered again and went to the Fifth District police station to question them, and the shouts were thunderous. The police and security team came out to suppress them, and improper measures caused this unfortunate incident. I deeply regret it. However, those present at the time included Mr. Yang Youren from the labor community and members of the Sixth District Party Department of the Party Department, which was nearby. Both sides witnessed the course of events and came forward to mediate and explain. Therefore, when dealing with it according to law in the future, they can also serve as third-party witnesses. After this incident occurred, the municipal government immediately dismissed You Bolu, the Fifth District Chief, from his post for investigation, and sent Section Chief Qi Tiecheng, Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng, Mr. Wu Kaixian from the Municipal Party Department, and Mr. Hou Dachun from the labor union to rush to the scene of the incident to investigate the facts. The local court was notified to send personnel to examine the two deceased, and the five injured were sent to the hospital. On the one hand, the families of the deceased were sought to claim the bodies, but no one had claimed them by this afternoon. Since this incident was caused by the military police and the Sixth District Party Department was also present, it was decided that the party, government, and military would jointly investigate the matter thoroughly. After the investigation is confirmed and the three parties report together, if the fault lies with the Fifth District, whether it is excessive defense or improper measures, it will definitely be dealt with severely according to law to punish dereliction of duty and apologize to the citizens. In short, I will absolutely handle this matter openly and impartially. The position of the Fifth District Chief will be temporarily maintained by transferring staff from other districts, and a formal appointment will be made soon. (Note by the reporter: The Public Security Bureau has transferred Wang Zhijing, the Second District Chief, to succeed him.)

Corpse Examination: After the municipal government learned of this incident the night before last, it immediately notified President Shen of the local court and Chief Prosecutor Liu by telephone, requesting them to handle the matter. Prosecutor Yang Wenjun was immediately appointed to lead Police Chief Xu Jinqing, Police Officer Chen Xihui, and supervising police officers Xu Guoguang, Zou Zhendong, Li Jiajun, Wang Xiqing, Zhang Chunsen, Yu Shaoshan, and Hu Xianglin to rush to the front of the Fifth District Police Station at midnight to conduct an inspection and suppress the riot. Inspector Shen found in front of the police station a person wearing a gray serge gown. The injured part was from the left cheek, out of the right temple. However, a pistol was inserted into the waistband. On the opposite side, there was a man wearing a blue short shirt and pants, barefoot. The bullet entered from the back and exited the front chest. Both corpses were in their twenties. The judge then ordered the collection of the bodies. When asked about the guns, Director You of the district claimed that the police officers had found two bullet casings, which they thought were fired by the deceased. The prosecutor then inspected the gun, the number of which was 5589, with three bullets inside, but not loaded. According to the usage of pistols, anyone who has fired a bullet will definitely load one later. Now, the gun barrel is covered with rust, and the gun is inserted in the waistband, which is very puzzling. Therefore, it was ordered that the pistol be filed for future summons of all relevant persons for thorough investigation and handling.

Family Members Petition: The two male corpses who were shot and killed on the spot the night before last, the younger of the two, were claimed by his biological mother yesterday morning. She claimed that she is currently a maid in a mansion. The deceased was her son, Shen Wanlin, 18 years old, from Shaoxing. He used to be an apprentice in the Dali Clothing Factory near Baoshan Road. He went out to play after work that night and suddenly this disaster occurred. She cried bitterly, and the situation was extremely tragic. At about 10 a.m. yesterday, she, along with the general public, went to the Sixth District Party Department to petition. The members of the Party Department, Yang Youren, etc., persuaded her, expressing that the Party Department stood on the position of urging the government to uphold justice impartially. In addition to the fact that member Yang Youren had personally reported the incident to Mayor Zhang Qun, Standing Committee members of the Municipal Party Department Pan Gongzhan, Wu Kaixian, and member Chen Xizeng, he has now submitted a request to the Municipal Party Department to punish the murderers. As for the other corpse, no one has claimed it yet.

Joint Investigation: This case has been jointly investigated by representatives from the party, government, and military. The representative of the Party Department is Wu Kaixian, the representative of the municipal government is Yu Hongjun, and the representative of the garrison command is Jiang Yi. Yesterday morning at 9 a.m., they went to the Fifth District Police Station to conduct an on-site inspection and personally inquired about the situation from the patrol officers and police officers at the time, and whether it was necessary to open fire. At 4 p.m., they gathered the civilian witnesses who were at the scene at the Sixth District Party Department and questioned the shopkeepers in the vicinity in detail. Regarding the claim of the Public Security Bureau that a gunshot was first heard among the crowd, all witnesses unanimously denied it. As for a pistol found on the corpse, someone also testified that after the special curfew was imposed in the Baoshan Road area, there were no pedestrians on the road. Someone on the upper floor personally saw plainclothes police officers groping under the mat shed covering the corpse for a long time. It was not until about 6 p'clock that they dispersed. According to Yu Hongjun to this newspaper reporter, the joint investigation has not yet been completed (it is scheduled to continue tomorrow, which is today). It is not yet time to publish it. Everything will be handled publicly in the future.

Voluntary Request for Punishment: Chen Xizeng, Chief of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, submitted a document to Mayor Zhang yesterday, stating, "Reporting matter: It is hereby reported that at 8 p.m. on the 1st of this month, a conflict occurred between residents near Baoshan Road in the Fifth District and the district police, resulting in a shooting that caused death. The details of the incident have been reported in person and reported in the newspaper. This case has been ordered to be suspended from duty pending investigation. As the director in charge, although the situation was urgent this time, it was also due to the lack of supervision and exhortation on weekdays. Therefore, I should sincerely request strict punishment to show a warning. In addition to strictly ordering my subordinates to deal with it carefully, I should prepare a document and submit it. This paper is for your convenience. Sincerely presented to Mayor Zhang."

Reporting by Delegation: Feng Xiancheng, Standing Committee Member of the Sixth District Party Department, and Yang Youren, Propaganda Committee Member, told reporters yesterday that they had reported the witnessed circumstances to the Municipal Party Department, stating, "At about 6 p.m. yesterday, two post office mail carriers came to the district headquarters to report that the Fifth District Public Security Bureau police officers had a conflict because they did not allow soldiers from the Fifth Team of the Railway Artillery Brigade to post anti-Japanese slogans, and took them to the district headquarters. At that time, hundreds of people followed behind and gathered at the door of the Fifth District, unwilling to disperse. Please go to investigate," etc. At that time, the District Party Department was preparing to convene a meeting to organize an anti-Japanese national salvation dare-to-die team. Xiancheng, Youren, and comrade Wen Ren'an went to the Fifth District to meet Guo Chenggai, a member of the district. According to him, the police officers were planning to deal with the matter according to law and could be dismissed tomorrow. The soldiers of the company were also satisfied when they heard this, so they stood on the top of the car at the door of the Public Security Bureau and reported to the audience and left. Some of the people had already dispersed, and another part chased and gathered in the Party Department in this district, waiting for the results of the negotiations. Later, Fu Jisan, a soldier on duty in the artillery team, and Yang Youren did their best to persuade them, and they also dispersed one after another. Xiancheng and others thought that the matter was over, so they planned to hold a meeting. Unexpectedly, at about 8 p.m., more than ten people came to report, stating that more than a thousand people were still gathered at the entrance of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau, unwilling to leave. Xiancheng, Youren, etc. went to the police station again. Those who went with them at that time included Zhu Jiujiu, Ge Yongqing, Li Qiuxin, Shi Tifen, Zhang Wenkui, and other comrades. After inquiring about the situation, they learned that three Japanese had been staying in the police station for an hour three hours before the conflict between the military and police. They asked the district chief to explain the ins and outs. Then Xiancheng introduced You Bolu to the crowd and gave a speech to explain the ins and outs. Xiancheng and Youren continued to explain to the crowd and asked everyone to disperse. At that time, a bus (from North Station to Jiangwan) also stopped at the door to listen. Shi Tifen, the chief auditor of the company, urgently ordered it to leave, and the people also ordered it to leave, but the machine had stopped and could not start. Later, for some reason, there was a conflict with the people. The driver of the car, Wu Decai, was beaten by the crowd and rescued by Shi Tifen to the Fifth District Police Station. At that time, Youren saw that the people were not dispersing, so he inserted himself into the crowd and persuaded them to disperse. Xiancheng then ordered Xu Ziqing, the traffic officer of the district headquarters, to go to the Fifth Company quickly, planning to ask the soldiers of the company to come and explain again and persuade everyone to disperse, so as to maintain order. He also sent Youren's hat in the hand of the traffic officer to Youren, and he was also in the middle of the crowd. At this time, You Bolu, the director of the Fifth District Police Station, ordered to open fire. The first order was issued, but the police did not open fire. The director jumped and shouted to open fire, so they fired live ammunition (Li Qiuxin and Zhang Wenkui saw it personally and can testify), firing at the crowd in a sweeping manner for about twenty shots. There were a large number of people at that time. Youren was squeezed towards the entrance of Beilian Zhili, and Xiancheng was also squeezed into the hardware store opposite the police station. After the gunshots, one person was killed about two or three feet away from where Xiancheng and Youren were located, and one person was killed on the opposite side. After Cheng saw it, he went to the police station, intending to question You Bolu, but You Bolu said, "You are being used by others, I will take care of things myself," etc., and went straight to the side. Xiancheng thought that the district chief was unreasonable, so he reported directly to the superior.

The Credit of the China Industrial Bank is Evident

Daily Rumors Mislead Citizens

The Bank Extends the Cashing Time

The Run on the Bank Gradually Subsided Last Night

The China Industrial Bank and its branches in this city experienced a run on the bank yesterday. The reason was that the Shanghai Nichinichi Shimbun, a Japanese newspaper, published inaccurate news yesterday. The holders of the tickets did not know the truth, so they went to the bank to exchange them yesterday morning and afternoon. However, the bank's accumulated funds were substantial, and those who went to exchange them were able to exchange cash and leave satisfied. According to the bank's regulations, foreign exchange will be stopped after 5 p.m. every day. Yesterday, in order to show its credit, it posted a notice at the door, stating that the office hours would be extended to 8 p.m. The notice said: "Our bank will extend its office hours to 8 p.m. today and will open early at 8 a.m. tomorrow morning (that is, this morning)." As a result, those who went to exchange gradually retreated, and by 7 o'clock, it had returned to its original state, which was no different from usual. It also shows that the bank's credit is evident and the rumor-mongers' efforts are exhausted.

Flew in by Ford Airplane This Afternoon

Mr. Gu Weijun, carrying the orders of Deputy Commander Zhang, flew from Ping to Beijing by Ford airplane to discuss diplomatic policies towards Japan. He met with Chairman Chiang in Beijing yesterday morning to report everything in detail and talked for a long time. At about 4 p.m. yesterday, Gu flew to Shanghai by Ford airplane and went straight back to his residence on Maigen Road to rest. He will still go to Beijing to discuss matters within days. The call for Gu to serve as the Minister of Foreign Affairs and the British Ambassador is also being brewed.
