Songhu Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui arrived in Shanghai by overnight express train from Beijing at 8 a.m. yesterday and got off at Zhenru. Jiang Yi, the director of the Deputy Adjutant Office of the Garrison Command, and others went to the station to greet him. After Xiong got off the car, he went straight back to his private residence and did not go to the Longhua Garrison Command to work in the afternoon.

Layman Lin Yin

Destroys His Home to Help Disaster Relief

Sells Property and Gets More Than 220,000

Uses 200,000 to Relieve Flood Disasters

The Chinese and Foreign Relief Society received a letter from someone named Layman Lin Yin yesterday, along with 200,000 yuan to help relief efforts. The country is in a difficult time, and the disaster is urgent. To resist foreign insults, we must first stabilize the country. The urgency of disaster relief is as urgent as a fire. We have this great philanthropist who destroys his home to help disaster relief. Raising his voice, I believe there will be responders. This is not only good news for the 30 million disaster victims, but also ironclad proof that people's hearts have not died. The original letter is attached below:

Respected Sirs, I have been living in seclusion in the mountains, isolated from the world, for many years. However, there is still a line of connection that cannot be completely severed, that is, my children send me the Shanghai Daily News every day. My children are filial and caring, afraid that I will be lonely in the deep mountains, so they use newspapers to relieve my boredom, and I cannot bear to refuse. Although the newspapers sent have been accumulating for a long time, I have never opened them to read them. They are all tied up and put on the shelf. These days, I have been sitting quietly, uneasy, and my heart is fluctuating. I feel that my mind is not pure, and my dregs are not exhausted. I have been arrogant in imagining introspection to blame myself. On the one hand, I still sincerely calm down and belittle myself in many ways, but I still cannot stop it. I picked up a bundle of newspapers and opened them to read them, to relieve my tense thoughts. Unexpectedly, various newspapers detailed the floods in various parts of the southern province, the water and fire, and the fierce disasters. There are also Hu Wenhu, a great philanthropist, who donated Tiger Balm, Headache Powder, Bagua Dan, and Qingkuai Water, and other medicines and huge donations, and overseas Chinese and domestic philanthropists enthusiastically recognized the donations to save the catastrophe. I live in seclusion in a secluded valley, and I cannot help but be shocked when I hear of this tragic situation. I believe that the restlessness of my heart these days is actually the compassion of my Buddha, silently showing the truth of saving people and saving myself. Only our generation adheres to the words "form" and "emptiness", but we still cannot stand idly by and watch people die. Therefore, I resolutely supported my cane down the mountain and discussed with my wife and children to relieve the suffering of the family. Fortunately, my wife and children did not refuse, unanimously agreed, and urged me to carry out disaster relief as if I were fighting a fire. I have sold all my thin property, earning more than 229,800 yuan. In addition to withdrawing more than 29,800 yuan for the cost of my wife's old age and the children's share, I intend to ask my friends to remit the remaining 200,000 yuan to the contribution meeting to meet the needs of disaster relief. I have always admired your association for its efforts in disaster relief over the years. The true donations are not falsely spent, and the actual benefits are for the disaster victims. Countless people have been saved. The whole country has a reputation for it. There is no religious discrimination or political influence. However, since I have gradually thinned out, I know that a drop in the bucket will not help the salary. I hope that Chinese and foreign philanthropists will appreciate my foolish sincerity, hear the wind and rise up. We must know that this disaster is a catastrophe that is rare in the ages. All of us Chinese people should jointly rise up and do our best to maintain it, so that the survivors after the disaster can slightly preserve their vitality. I hope that the great philanthropists of your association will hold the heart of hunger and drowning, and call for help from the high ground, so that it is not difficult to build a tower by accumulating sand and to make a robe by collecting armpits, so that tens of millions of disaster victims who are waiting to be slaughtered can be reborn. When I am in the mountains, I should pray for the great philanthropists day and night, without end. After I have finished my worldly affairs, I will return to the mountains immediately, and from now on my heart will be clear and cool, I will not deal with worldly affairs, and I will never set foot in the world again. Sincerely to the kind gentlemen of the Chinese and Foreign Relief Society, Lin Yin bows and says goodbye. In addition, I continue to see in the daily newspapers that the floods in Jiangbei are extremely serious, and the accumulated water is not receding. It is difficult to express the situation. Is it possible to transfer my donation to Jiangbei? It is now urgent to drain the accumulated water and use work as a substitute for disaster relief, so that both sides will benefit and the disaster victims will have hope of survival, so that the spring plowing next year will not be without harvest. I also ask all the good people to pay attention to this. If my intention is not feasible, please let your association allocate it as needed. And again,

Baoshan Dike Protection Association

Requests Thorough Investigation of Dike Works

The sea dikes in Baoshan County were attacked by storms and tides, and the entire dike was in danger everywhere. The Jiangsu Provincial Government quickly allocated huge sums of money and ordered the Jiangnan Dike Works Office to rescue them quickly. It has been half a month. Recently, Xue Zhaoshu, the director of the Jiangnan Dike Works Office, reported to the provincial government on the rescue situation, saying that since the dike was in danger, more than 100 workers have been hired every day to work separately, and the rescue project has been completed by 80%. When the dike protection committee of the county heard the news, it immediately sent many members to the dike to conduct an on-site investigation. It was found that there were 23 workers working in the Wuyuedun section, 17 in Chenhuabin, more than 40 in Zhangjiazha, more than 130 in Xuejiatan, and less than 30% of the earth bags. There were more than 20 in Niantoujing, and less than 10% of the earth bags. In addition, no one was working. The total number of workers was only more than 200. The rescue project was less than half completed, and most of it was done hastily. The dike protection committee found that the results of the above-mentioned survey were greatly inconsistent with those reported by the Jiangnan Dike Works Office. It was obvious that Director Xue of the office only sought personal gain and falsely reported to the provincial government. The dike is still in danger. If it is breached, not only will the lives and property of the entire Baoshan County be turned into nothing, but Shanghai will also perish. In addition, Taiga and other counties will inevitably be affected. After immediately convening a meeting of all members for discussion, the crowd was indignant. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to Shen Baixian, the director of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, about Director Xue's false report, requesting a thorough investigation to ensure that the work is real and the money is not wasted, so as to protect the lives of the people in the county.

Zhang Xilin Kidnapped

The Car Was Found Near Guanghua University

Zhang Xilin, a local, opened the Lishengchang Store at No. 147-8 Shandong Road, specializing in silk threads and factory silk business for more than ten years. At about 7 p.m. last night, Zhang took his own chartered car from outside to the store, preparing to dine. When he walked to the middle of the store, he was taking off his gown and had not yet sat down. Two kidnappers suddenly came from outside the door, wearing blue cloth shirts and pants, and holding pistols. They mixed into the store, dragged Zhang out, and tied him to car No. 8381, which was parked near the Sino-Western Pharmacy. Then they drove straight south, turned west at Avenue Edward VII, and disappeared in an instant. After reporting to the Central Patrol Room in charge, they immediately sent detectives to investigate. About an hour later, car No. 8381 was found near Guanghua University on the newly built Da West Road outside the boundary. It is said that the car is a small Austin brand, black in color, and owned by Mr. Wang. At the time of the incident, the driver drove it out, and the driver did not know where he went. Zhang Xilin is 51 years old and lives on Beile Road in the French Concession. When the bandits went to kidnap him, there were six in total, two bandits were on guard outside the door, and two bandits were in the car.

Downstairs in the New Customs Building

Thieves Steal and Injure People

Stabbed Severely After Leaving the Store

2,500 Yuan Stolen

Jin Yongfa, a native of Changshu, an employee of the Xinfu Foreign Firm at No. 9 Avenue Edward VII, was ordered to take 2,500 yuan in banknotes to the cashier's office on the fourth floor of the New Customs Building at about 4 p.m. yesterday. Unexpectedly, as soon as Jin arrived downstairs in the New Customs Building, five thugs who had been ambushing there rushed forward as soon as they saw Yongfa, stabbing him in the abdomen with a knife, causing his large intestine to flow out. He was also stabbed three times in both hands and three times in the chest. He was robbed of 2,500 yuan and then they all ran away. Later, the Central Patrol Room No. 1671 and No. 1308 arrived and sent the injured person to Renji Hospital for treatment. The situation of the robbery was reported to the head of the patrol room, and he ordered Chinese and Western detectives to investigate the murderers and punish them severely.

Ten Thousand Dollars

A Massive Fraud Case Involving Warehouse Receipts

The Futai Exchange Was Also Defrauded of Four Thousand Dollars

The Handwriting and Seals Were No Different From Before

The Tongyi Trust Company at 126 Beijing Road had unconditionally deposited public bond warehouse receipts worth 100,000 yuan with the Wenzhou Fuzi Exchange. On August 31st, they received a letter from Fuzi in Wenzhou stating that someone would be sent to retrieve the warehouse receipts. The next day, a man claiming to be Zhu Ming arrived and the receipts were handed over in full. Unexpectedly, they then received a telegram from Wenzhou Fuzi stating that the exchange's documents and seals had suddenly been lost and requesting that the warehouse receipts be carefully guarded and all payments stopped. Tongyi immediately telegraphed back, saying that Zhu Ming had already taken them in full. The exchange then sent someone to Shanghai to investigate the truth and learned that

Dai Dingfu From Wenzhou Was Highly Suspected in This Case and Was Planning to Sell the Receipts in Hangzhou, So the Informant Lin Shoumei Went to Hangzhou to Arrest Dai. At the same time, Xu Bohua was also arrested, but after questioning, Xu was found to be uninvolved and was released on the spot. Dai was then escorted to the First Special District Court in Shanghai and confessed that the masterminds behind the case were Zeng Liulin and Zhu Xiang, who were staying in Room 511 of the Dongya Hotel on Nanjing Road. When the police went to arrest them, Zeng and Zhu were not there. Xu Bohua, who had been arrested and released in Hangzhou, and several others from Wenzhou, including Zhao Luoshu, Chen Susheng, and Chen Yuanyao, were arrested and brought to court. After an initial interrogation, Zhao, Chen, and Chen were released as they were found to be uninvolved. The court also sent a letter to the Wenzhou District Court to investigate whether the Jincheng Exchange had commissioned Dai Dingfu to contact the Zhongnan and Yanyue Banks in Shanghai for business (as Dai had claimed to be commissioned by the exchange to come to Shanghai for business). The Tongyi Trust Company and the managers of the Futai Exchange, which had also been defrauded, were summoned to court for questioning. Yesterday was the court date, and Judge Jiang Gongliang presided over the trial. Dai Dingfu testified that he was 21 years old, from Wenzhou, and worked at an exchange. He was arrested in Hangzhou because the police said that

Zeng Liulin Had Defrauded Public Bonds Because I Knew Him and Was Suspected of Being Involved, But I Did Not Know the Details. At this point, the police lawyer stated that Dai Dingfu had been arrested in Hangzhou. He had met Zeng Liulin in Shanghai, and Zeng had asked him to contact the Agricultural and Industrial Bank in Hangzhou to sell bond receipts, giving him 500 yuan as entertainment expenses. The informant, Lin Shoumei, manager of the Wenzhou Fuzi Exchange, learned of this and reported it to the authorities, leading to his arrest. As for Xu Bohua, the Wenzhou Shanghai Fellow Villagers Association and the Wenzhou Junior Public Middle School sent letters of support, stating that Xu was not involved in the case and had a profession.

There Were Only Two Suspicious Points (1) When He Was in the Police Station, He Claimed to Be Unemployed and Was With Zeng, Seeking Work. (2) Zeng Liulin Arrived in Shanghai First, and Xu Came Later. Why Was Xu Arrested and Released in Hangzhou, Only to Be Arrested Again at Zeng's Place in Shanghai? According to Xu Bohua, he was an accountant at the Wenzhou Public Middle School. He came to Shanghai to purchase instruments for the school. He arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou on August 28th and met Zeng Liulin while matching goods at the Shixue Tongyi Hall. They had previously been introduced by Zeng to a dentist and were fellow villagers. Since arriving in Shanghai, he had been staying at the Xiangbin Hotel, where many fellow villagers from Wenzhou stayed. Zeng also came to see him there. He arrived in Shanghai on the same boat as Dai. The police lawyer then stated that when Xu was arrested in Hangzhou,

He Was Questioned and Released Because He Was Found to Be Uninvolved. At That Time, the Informant Lin Shoumei Returned to Shanghai After Arresting Dai Dingfu in Hangzhou, and Xu Followed on the Same Train, Going Directly to the Dongya Hotel to Report to Zeng Liulin. This Behavior Was Highly Suspicious. When Questioned, Xu Stated That He Had Visited Me in Shanghai, But I Had Gone to Visit Him, So He Was Arrested Unexpectedly. Next, Li Wenjie, the representative of the Tongyi Trust Company, stated that they had dealings with the Wenzhou Fuzi Exchange. Previously, they had unconditionally deposited 50,000 yuan in reorganization warehouse receipts and 50,000 yuan in 19th year rehabilitation warehouse receipts, totaling 100,000 yuan, with the company. On August 31st, they received a letter from the Wenzhou Fuzi Exchange dated the 27th, stating that the receipts were needed for other purposes and that Zhu Ming had been entrusted to retrieve them. The next day, Zhu Ming arrived with another letter and a business card. After examining the

Letter and Handwriting and Seals, The Tone Was the Same as Previous Letters and the Most Recent Letter. They Trusted Him and Handed Them Over on the Spot. Unexpectedly, After the Payment Was Made, They Suddenly Received a Telegram From Fuzi in the Afternoon Stating That the Seal Was Lost and the Bond Receipts Should Not Be Paid, But It Was Too Late. Moreover, Zhu Ming Said Before Leaving That the Government Would Repay the Principal and Interest of the Bond Receipts at the End of the Month, Which Could Be Done Through the Futai Exchange, Amounting to Over a Thousand Yuan. Because They Knew That the Two Companies Had Dealings With Each Other and Had Always Done Things This Way, It Made People Even More Unsuspecting. The Means of Deception Were Very Meticulous. Next, Jin Runfu, the agent of the Futai Exchange, stated that they had dealings with Fuzi. Before This Incident Occurred, There Was a Debt of One or Two Thousand. On August 28th, They Received a Letter From Fuzi Stating That Chen Shouqing Had Been Specially Sent to Withdraw 4,000 Yuan. The Next Day, Someone Claiming to Be Chen Arrived to Withdraw the Money. The Handwriting and Seals Were No Different From Past Dealings, Making It Impossible to Detect the Fraud.

Therefore, They Paid Without Suspicion. Later, They Received a Telegram From Fuzi and Realized That They Had Been Defrauded, But the Payment Had Already Been Made. They Had No Choice But to Telegraph Back, Saying That It Had Been Referred. At This Time, the Police Lawyer Requested That the Four Letters of Withdrawal Be Handed Over to the Police to Check the Handwriting, Because Xu and Dai Had Written Confessions in the Police Station That Could Be Compared. Whether to Prosecute the Escaped Zeng Liulin and Zhu Xiang Would Be Resolved at the Next Court Hearing, Because It Was the Police's Usual Practice to Only File Charges After the Defendant Was Apprehended. At This Point, the Court Adjourned the Hearing and Summoned the Plaintiff Lin Shoumei to Attend the Trial.

The Pacific Conference Will Open as Scheduled

A Preparatory Meeting Will Be Held in Shanghai Starting on the 12th

Formal Conference Representatives Will Not Be Allowed to Attend

The Japanese Military's Invasion of the Northeast Will Be Discussed

The Fourth Conference of the Pacific International Academic Association, originally scheduled to be canceled due to the Japanese military's invasion of the Eastern Provinces, has recently been encouraged by the Central Government. Yesterday morning, our preparatory committee held a meeting and decided to proceed with the conference as originally scheduled, from the 21st of this month to the 4th of November, in Hangzhou. It was also decided to hold a preparatory meeting in Shanghai for one week starting on the 12th of this month. As for the issue of Japanese representatives attending the conference, after repeated discussions between Mr. Green, the American representative and chairman of the conference, and other representatives from Britain, France, Canada, etc., it has been decided that they will only attend the preparatory meeting and not the formal conference. Regarding the issues to be discussed, in addition to the case of the Japanese military

Page 16

Committing Atrocities in the Northeast, Which Will Be the Subject of Extremely Important Discussions, It Has Also Been Decided to Discuss the Overall Theme. Furthermore, when representatives from Britain, the United States, Canada, and other countries arrived in Shanghai aboard the British ship Empress of Canada, the American side immediately sent a representative named Lao Kao to Liaoning to investigate the Japanese military's atrocities in order to gather information for the conference's discussion of the Manchurian case. Yesterday, it was learned that the representative had already arrived in Shenyang and would continue to investigate in Jilin and Changchun. However, according to a reporter from the New Sound News Agency who visited Mr. Massey, the former Canadian Prime Minister and a representative attending the conference, the day before yesterday, Mr. Massey said that he was unaware of this matter and did not wish to express his opinion on the Manchurian incident.

Smooth Communication of Wired Telegraphs Between Shanghai-Fuzhou and Shanghai-Hankou

The Quzhou Telegraph Bureau Installs Fast Telegraph Machines to Assist Telegraphing

Telegraph Transmission Between Fujian and Guangdong Is Very Fast

The Direct Line Between Shanghai and Hankou Has Also Been Repaired

In April of this year, after our country recovered the Xiamen Gulangyu submarine cable of the Great Eastern and Great Northern Telegraph Companies, the Shanghai-Fuzhou direct land line of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau on Sichuan Road in this city suddenly became busy. This was because all telegrams sent from Shanghai to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Quanzhou, Hanjiang, and the two Guang provinces were relayed through this line. In addition, international telegrams sent from various countries to Fujian and Guangdong, which used to be relayed by submarine cable companies, are now routed through the land line due to the recovery of submarine cable sovereignty. The volume is even greater than before. However, the line passes through the entire province of Zhejiang to Fuzhou, which is too long, and it is old and prone to damage, causing frequent disruptions in work. In view of this, and in order to maintain our country's telegraph reputation to the outside world after recovering telegraph sovereignty, the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau specially requested and obtained approval from the Ministry of Communications to allocate funds to order the Shanghai-Fuzhou Telegraph Main Line Works Bureau to carry out major repairs, and ordered the Shanghai Telecommunications Machinery Manufacturing Plant to configure fast telegraph machines to assist telegraphing and install them in the Quzhou Telegraph Bureau. At present, the line repair project has been completed, and the auxiliary motor of the Quzhou Telegraph Bureau has also been connected. Recently, news from the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau on Sichuan Road stated that the Shanghai-Fuzhou line has been extremely smooth since the major repairs and the installation of the auxiliary motor. In the past, it could only send 40 to 50 telegrams per hour, but now it can send 150 to 160 telegrams. The speed and capacity have increased more than threefold, and the telegraph signals are clear and there are very few errors. The merchants and people from Fujian and Guangdong stationed in Shanghai are all very satisfied.

It is also reported that the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau's direct line to Hankou was previously disrupted by the floods in Hankou, as well as the flooding along the Yangtze River, such as in Wuhu and Jiujiang, which damaged many telegraph poles and made it impossible to repair them for a time. Now that the floodwaters have receded, Tao, the chief engineer of the Shanghai-Hankou Telegraph Main Line Works Bureau, personally went to Wuhu, Jiujiang, Daye, and other places to inspect the damage and supervise the engineers and line workers to rush to repair it day and night. It was restored to its original state yesterday morning (the 2nd). The Shanghai-Hankou direct fast machine dual-operation work has resumed. Since Hankou was devastated by the floods, the market has almost collapsed. After the floodwaters receded, the restoration of the Hankou market and telecommunications is particularly important. The bureau has carefully reorganized the telegraph services in Hankou and other places, all with the premise of assisting commercial development and facilitating the people.

Memorial Service for Chiang Wei-shui of Taiwan Tomorrow

Location: Penglai Movie Theater, Xiaoximen, Shanghai

The Shanghai All Circles Commemorate Mr. Chiang Wei-shui of Taiwan Preparatory Committee Public Announcement: Mr. Chiang Wei-shui of Taiwan led the people of Taiwan in engaging in the national liberation movement for twenty years. His purpose was to seek freedom and equality for the people. Although he suffered the oppression and imprisonment of Japanese imperialism, his revolutionary spirit was never diminished. His name will be eternally recorded in the revolutionary history of Taiwan. Unfortunately, the tragic news came that Mr. Chiang passed away in Taiwan at 7:30 a.m. on August 5th. The loss of such a great teacher is a great loss to the future of national liberation for the revolutionary people of Taiwan. All our revolutionary comrades at home and abroad should also deeply mourn. Therefore, it has been decided to hold a memorial service for Mr. Chiang at 9:00 a.m. on October 4th at the Penglai Movie Theater in Penglai Market, Xiaoximen, Shanghai City (the Huajie 2nd and 3rd Road roundabout trams all reach the front door). At that time, we respectfully hope that you will send elegiac scrolls and send representatives to enthusiastically participate in order to console the departed martyr and encourage those who follow. This is our earnest request. Please send elegiac items to Mr. Zhuang Xiquan, Zhuang Chuncheng Firm, No. 7 Jiuxingli, Xinkaihe, French Concession, Shanghai for forwarding.

Wang Zhengting Arrived in Shanghai by Ship Yesterday

Proceeding Directly to the Hospital for Long-Term Recuperation

Former Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Zhengting arrived in Shanghai aboard the Yongshui warship from Beijing at 11:00 a.m. yesterday, landing at the Gaochangmiao Naval Dock. He was accompanied by Mrs. Wang, Ms. Shi Meili, and others. Yang Nianzu, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, personally went to the dock to take care of him. After landing, Wang proceeded directly to the hospital by car for recuperation. It is reported that the injury has almost completely healed and only requires rest.

The Harbor Quarantine Station Issues

Report No. 10 on the Prevention of Cholera

The Harbor Quarantine Station issued Report No. 10 on the prevention of cholera in Shanghai yesterday, stating: (1) During the week from September 20th to September 26th, the cholera situation in this city has not changed much. According to the survey, the report is as follows: There were 38 cases of cholera in the Chinese area this week, with 3 deaths. There were 29 cases in the Public Concession (including 1 foreigner), with 3 deaths. There were 7 cases in the French Concession (including 1 foreigner), with 3 deaths. (Including foreigners) In total, there were 74 cases and 9 deaths last week. According to the above situation, the cholera epidemic is likely to gradually disappear in the near future. (2) The Wusong Quarantine Hospital of this station still has 1 cholera recovery patient. In the past week, ships from Hankou have been thoroughly inspected and no suspected cholera patients have been found. Therefore, the number of patients in the Wusong Quarantine Hospital has not increased. However, in order to prevent the epidemic, passengers from Hankou to Shanghai are vaccinated against cholera when boarding in Hankou. When arriving at Wusong, they are re-examined by the medical officers of this station. Those who have not been vaccinated are given vaccinations at any time. (3) Director Wu Liande took the Gonghe wheel to Hankou on the morning of September 26 to inspect the epidemic situation in the flood-stricken areas in order to plan epidemic prevention and harbor quarantine measures. After Wu returns to Shanghai, he will definitely have new methods for preventing cholera to contribute to society and the public.

In addition to ordering the department to refer to it and start planning, this letter is specially replied to, so please take note.

The Shanghai Guangdong Guild Hall and the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Business Federation rescued fellow villagers from the Hankou disaster area who came to Shanghai. The Oriental Review Weekly, which has been in preparation for a long time and was founded by well-known people in this city, was published today. The content is very rich and includes many anti-Japanese articles. It is quite brilliant. Those who subscribe for half a year have the hope of receiving hundreds of yuan in gifts.

The Hongkou Epidemic Hospital Extends Its Closing Date

Since its opening this year, the Hongkou Epidemic Hospital in Yinxiang District has been crowded with patients, with more than 100 outpatients every day, resulting in a large budget overrun. It was originally scheduled to close at the end of September to prepare for the construction of permanent hospital buildings. However, it received a letter from the Bureau of Health stating that the epidemic situation this year is more serious and must be extended to October 15th to avoid the risk of cholera patients having nowhere to go for treatment. It is now reported that the hospital has agreed to do its best.

The Ya Ge Troupe Will Perform the Play "Down With Snobbery" Tomorrow Night

In view of the current rampant violence of Japan, the Ya Ge Troupe has specially rehearsed a new play, "Snobbery," by Zhu Choushi and Wu Jiangfeng. The plot depicts snobs doing all kinds of evil in an incisive and thorough manner. In the end, they are overthrown. Tomorrow night, at the National Road City Exhibition, the troupe will be invited to perform this play. This is also a manifestation of fulfilling the national duty, awakening compatriots, and jointly relieving the national crisis.

China Now Has Chemical Porcelain Products

Chemical porcelain products used to be imported from the West, resulting in a huge annual outflow. There was no alternative. The Science Instrument Museum contacted Jingdezhen two years ago and, after many setbacks, finally succeeded. The first batch of Bunsen electromagnetic cylinders has been shipped and is of better quality and glaze than imported products. The second batch of mortar samples has also arrived and has been tested and found to be suitable. The remaining products, such as evaporating dishes, crucibles, and various items for sericulture, are also being studied. This is indeed good news for promoting domestic products.

Survey Statistics of the Value and Types of Japanese Imports

Table

The Japanese invaders are rampant, and the whole country is indignant. Patriots from all walks of life are boiling with enthusiasm and rising up to carry out the movement to save the country and resist Japan. As it stands, before the National Government decides on a policy, boycotting enemy goods is indeed the only passive weapon to punish the Japanese invaders. Most of Japan's surplus production ends up in our country's market, accounting for more than one-third of our country's imports. The total value of Japanese goods imported in the last three years is staggering. If Chinese goods were shipped to Japan in such quantities, the Japanese would definitely be terrified and cry out about economic difficulties. According to the survey, the value of Japanese goods imported in 1928 was 334,757,417 taels (customs taels), equivalent to more than 500 million yuan in national currency. In 1929, it was 338,523,097 taels, equivalent to more than 505 million yuan in national currency. In 1930, it was 338,356,529 taels, equivalent to more than 505 million yuan in national currency. Therefore, the lifeblood of our nation has been unknowingly sucked dry by the Japanese. Even if they no longer treat us with inhumane cruelty, we should still make nationwide efforts to create products in order to recover the huge outflow. Now that the invaders have penetrated deeply and disaster is imminent, the boycott of goods must not be as lax as before. There should be a permanent plan of action. The first step must be to investigate the quantity, value, and types of Japanese goods imported. After the investigation is clear, Japanese goods exhibition halls and large-scale Japanese goods exhibitions should be set up in various places so that the public can know the true face of Japanese goods and avoid confusing them with domestic products. It can also provide a basis for the industrial sector to study and improve. It is reported that the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has completed the investigation and statistics of the quantity, value, and types of Japanese goods in the past three years and has produced statistics. We have obtained the full statistics of the investigation and will publish them in the newspaper day by day as follows.

Suggestions from Sha Bingruo (For. Japan. Four. Items.)

I have been reading your newspaper for days and have seen reports of the Japanese military's atrocities. We must awaken our compatriots and jointly face the national crisis. Your newspaper has always been known for its fairness and patriotism. I dare to propose the following four items, please publish them in the newspaper: (1) The Ministry of Education should order all bookstores to incorporate the Japanese military's atrocities into the textbooks of primary and secondary schools, so that the innocent and simple primary and secondary school students can recognize Japan and stimulate their patriotic feelings. (2) Please ask all bookstores to edit a large number of books on Japanese issues and reduce the price of books, such as The Manchurian Problem of Great East Asia, China's Twenty-Year Sino-Japanese Relations, and A Modern History of Japanese Imperialism's Aggression Against China, so that our fellow compatriots can also make an effort to purchase and read them. (3) Please ask all newspapers and magazines to announce and comment as much as possible on all Japanese actions and facilities if they are investigated, so as to give the people correct guidance. (4) Urge anti-Japanese associations not to slacken their work. (Reply) Will be published immediately

Miss Mou's Inquiry (Regarding Whether or Not to Sell Goods to the Japanese)

At this time when the Japanese bandits are displaying their martial prowess, the hearts of the entire nation are filled with indignation, and there is a unanimous call for economic severance with Japan. However, I have some doubts about this, and I would like to ask for your guidance, sir. I am currently working in a store in Hongkou. The owner is Chinese, and usually many Japanese people patronize it. Ever since those Japanese bandits seized the Northeast, the Chinese are furious and refuse to look at them. However, the Japanese bandits still patronize our business as usual. I would like to ask if we should continue to sell to them? If we sell, would it be a violation of economic severance?

(Reply) Since the people of the nation have declared economic severance, we should not sell goods to them. You should first explain this point to the store owner, and also agree with your colleagues to adopt a consistent attitude. It is important to be firm in your stance, but avoid causing disputes in language. This is crucial.

Mr. Jin Yeqiu's Inquiry (Proposing a Cloth Clothing Association)

Since the Japanese army occupied Shenyang, our compatriots have suffered this brutal experience. From now on, our lives should be simplified as much as possible. At this time, it is necessary to advocate wearing cloth clothing. The only effective way for India's Gandhi to subdue the British was to simplify his personal life and not use British goods. Chinese society has been accustomed to extravagance in recent years, and imported goods are highly regarded for daily necessities. Those who call themselves the intellectual class are especially fond of Western suits and leather shoes. The city admires the high, and all directions are higher by a foot. This trend has spread from cities to villages, without any limit. Therefore, the responsibility for changing the atmosphere lies with those of us who call ourselves the intellectual class. From now on, our youth should change to old cloth student uniforms to establish a national spirit of patriotism and supporting national goods. There are often people in society who judge others by their appearance, and regard those who wear plain clothes as ignorant villagers. This trend is especially prevalent in Shanghai. Therefore, before implementing the cloth uniform system, we should first unite several like-minded comrades and create an association to hang on the lapel, to express one's belief. The emblem of the association should be shield-shaped, with a depiction of Hou Yi shooting down the sun on the front, to show the object of one's efforts. On the back, write a simple warning, so that it is striking and does not become dull over time. This will make society respect those who wear cloth clothing and despise those who wear imported clothing. Such a change will have a very important and great impact on the country. I dare to ask the reporter to speak out loudly for this cause.

(Reply) Very good. We will publish your proposal. We also hope that everyone will start from themselves.

Miss Shao's Inquiry (Omitted) (Marriage Problems)

(Reply) After reading your letter, I deeply understand that your thoughts and actions are noble and pure. Now I give you three words: (1) Freedom of marriage is granted by current laws. Since there is nothing to be ashamed of, you can be completely unhesitating. (2) In everything you do, you should not be too hasty. When the water flows, the channel will be formed, and it will naturally be complete. (3) The sick body must be treated. Since you believe in religion, you should broaden your mind and vision, and eliminate the psychology of restraint and sorrow. A relaxed state of mind will have a very rapid impact on your physical health.

Free Talk

Heartbreaking Words

— Juan

Dear compatriots, there is a Western saying that goes "A tooth for a tooth, an eye for an eye." A tooth for a tooth and an eye for an eye means that if someone bites me, I will bite them back. If someone stares at me, I will stare back. This is originally a very fair method. But how do our Chinese people treat foreigners? If someone bites me, I just pat myself and let it go. If someone stares at me, I just lower my head and let it go. Even if a foreigner wants to slap my face, I offer my face to their hand. If a foreigner wants to chop off my head, I offer my head to their knife. Alas, this is called courtesy, this is called tolerance, this is called love of peace.

From The Unweeded Garden, Talks by Zhai Fu

A Thorough Cleaning

Someone asked me, "Why do you contribute to Free Talk?" I said, "I just love the word 'free' in its name." When I see Free Talk, I think of the freedom of children, the freedom of women, the freedom of oppressed people, and the freedom of small and weak nations around the world. Here, I want to fire the cannons of freedom, break the city of slavery, seize the weapons of the slave owners, and unshackle the slaves, so that no one will ever be a slave again, and everyone will become a free person. Someone says that slaves also have freedom. How so? Before becoming a slave, they must have the freedom to choose their path. Whether they fight and die as a free person or beg for survival as a slave of a conquered nation, in between, don't they have the freedom to choose? So, unless they are determined and willing to be slaves themselves, no one has the power to force them to be slaves. What we need to eradicate completely is this kind of slavish mentality. If this slavish mentality is not thoroughly eradicated, a world of freedom will never be realized. Good! Let's give it a thorough cleaning!

"Who has a pen of freedom?

Let's sweep together!

Until what day?

No slaves on the earth!"

The Painful Words of a Returnee from Shenyang

— Jiang Jianyi

My friend, Mr. Jiang Jianxing, works at the Shenyang Arsenal. He personally experienced the disaster of the Japanese Kou's attack on the city on the 19th. Yesterday, he returned south in disguise, having narrowly escaped death. He described the bestial atrocities of the Japanese army, which were hair-raising. I will now record three of the things he said.

When the Japanese army entered Shenyang, after successfully attacking the Beida Camp Arsenal, they disarmed all the police in the city at the same time. Then, guided by ronin, they rushed into people's homes like wolves and boars. They ordered stores to hang Japanese flags everywhere. Jiang was staying at his friend Mr. Guo's house at the time. Guo ran a general store in the business district and lived there with his family. On the morning of the 19th, amidst the sounds of gunfire, the Japanese army crowded into their house. Mr. Guo tried to avoid them, but the Japanese army dragged him out and ordered him to hang the Japanese flag immediately. He was unable to comply in such a rush. Then they kicked and beat him severely. Amidst his cries of pain, a bullet took his life. Jiang, along with Mr. Guo's elderly mother and family members, were taking the opportunity to escape when the Japanese army aimed at them from behind. Bullets rained down. The old mother tripped first. Mr. Guo did not even have time to see her. Jiang fell to the ground, injured his forehead, and his face was covered in blood. He barely escaped with his life. In his dazed state, he still heard the miserable screams of Mr. Guo's wife, who was being forced into a separate room. The sound was so terrible that it broke the hearts of those who heard it. Mr. Jiang said that he was weeping at the time, saying that if this hatred is not avenged, what is the point of wearing a head.

After the Japanese army began to kill on a large scale, corpses piled up in the streets, blocking the roads. The Japanese did not ask the reason and shot anyone wearing Chinese clothing on sight. Especially those wearing student uniforms and Zhongshan suits had no chance of survival. Mr. Jiang personally saw more than ten workers and students, dressed in work clothes and student uniforms, fleeing in panic, their faces pale. Later, the Japanese army chased after them. When they could no longer escape, they forced them to stand side by side against a wall and cursed at them in Japanese. Then, one by one, they were executed. Those who tried to escape were also shot and killed, none surviving. Mr. Jiang lay among the corpses, with the backs of the Japanese soldiers stepping over him. He said that even though he did not die, the pain and horror he witnessed were more agonizing than death itself.

Jiang's younger brother, Lingxiao, was studying at the highest institution of learning in the Northeast. On the night his school was surrounded, he first saw the flames of artillery fire lighting up the sky. The whole school was in chaos. Then he heard the sounds of killing shake the earth. The Japanese army surged towards them like a tide. Jiang's younger brother nearly fell victim to a sharp blade, and in his anger, he wanted to die. Later, he escaped to look for his brother. He has been separated from him since then. Jianxing fled to Huanggu Tun and saw his brother's classmate among the refugees. Only then did he learn that Lingxiao had escaped from the school. However, his whereabouts have been unknown since the scattering. It is likely that he was buried with his blood splashing on our lost land. Jianxing has an elderly mother who dotes on her youngest son. He said that since he escaped death, he often recalled the tragic sights of disembowelment, chest-stabbing, and corpses lying in pools of blood. He also remembered his younger brother. Alas, rather than be a weak slave, it is better to be a heroic ghost. I do not have time to mourn for Lingxiao, nor can I console Jianxing's grief. Moved, I wrote four poems: Ten thousand calamities have finally led to today's change. There is no place on earth where one can greedily cling to life. Singing and weeping are common occurrences. There must be people who shed blood on the battlefield. The earth shakes and the sky rumbles again this time. A broken body and a dead heart leave endless grief. Indeed, the methods are like those in Korea. Ten thousand heads cannot be exchanged for return. Painfully crying and pleading cannot bear to express all. How can this matter be empty talk? Carrying weapons and wearing armor, let us die on the sandy battlefield. It is not yet satisfying to have killed Japanese slaves. Weeping blood and piercing our hearts, we will never forget. Ten thousand people cry out, willing to die together. This is no longer a day for calmness and composure. Let us pull the strong bow and shoot the sun. (Moving to help with disaster relief)

The Enemy Tower in Muzhen for Destroying Japanese Pirates

— Zheng Yimei

The battlements still overlook the riverside. The small, fortified pass defends against the enemy.

Today, the smoke of war has long dissipated. The setting sun and fragrant grass face the remaining spring. This poem is by Wang Ruyu, praising the Muzhen Rescue Tower. The enemy tower is located at the end of the White Pagoda Bridge. It is more than thirteen zhang wide and three zhang six chi high. It is built on a foundation of stacked stones and the four sides are made of bricks. There are holes on the sides to fire arrows, stones, muskets, and cannons. I moored my boat in Xiangxi and once strolled beneath it. From there, one can see the beautiful scenery of Lingyan and Zhiqiu, which are close at hand, inspiring a desire to look up and emulate. It is truly a beautiful place. According to the county records, this tower was built during the Jiajing period of the Ming Dynasty by the Censor-in-Chief Shang Weizhi. It is one of the ten scenic spots of Muzhen. Legend has it that in the thirty-fourth year of Jiajing, Japanese pirates burned and looted almost everywhere from Fengqiao to Muzhen and the Western Mountains. The military commander Ren Huan and the commander-in-chief Tang Kewan led strong soldiers to fight them. The pirates fled into Taihu Lake and burned and looted both Dongting Mountains. Later, they harassed the Baodai Bridge again. They were surrounded by Ren Huan's troops. The pirates broke through the encirclement and crossed the Five Dragon Bridge, fleeing to Meiwang. The next day, they fled to Sangyan Mountain. Ren Huan searched and captured them, killing many pirates. This is the location of the enemy tower. After Ren Huan died, the residents built a temple for him in Zoumatang and sculpted his image to offer incense. They did not forget his great contribution in suppressing the pirates. Unfortunately, after the war, the temple image was changed and no longer resembled the original attire. At this time, when the East China Sea is turbulent and the pirates are committing atrocities, I wonder if there is a Ren Gong in this world. Even if I were to hold his whip, I would be willing. Ren Gong, styled Yinggan, from Anren. I specially record this to serve as a model for suppressing the Japanese pirates today.

The Chinese Peace-Loving People Who Blindly Believe in Justice

— Hu Jingping

Recently, apart from a few people who have realized that the word "justice" is not very reliable, the rest are still blindly believing in this intangible, invisible, and unrealizable "justice." We can see this from the fact that many people are still hoping that the League of Nations or the United States (or even Russia) will come out to help.

In my opinion, blindly believing in justice is a pompous word used to deceive oneself. In fact, it is precisely the cowardice of us Chinese.

Preliminary Discussion on the Fundamental Problems of Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation (3)

— Ji Ping

Boycotting Japanese goods is the most urgent task for China at present. As long as we work hard to boycott, I dare to predict that Japan will discover three terrifying phenomena in three years: (1) Large-scale industrial and commercial paralysis, leaving only a part to supply domestic demand. (2) Extreme economic panic due to industrial and commercial paralysis, which will inevitably lead to internal deterioration. (3) The people will confront the government, and political unrest will occur. At that time, Japanese imperialism will naturally tend to soften and change their ferocious face. Therefore, I say that the final victory will belong to us. However, boycotting Japanese goods is still a passive way to save the country. The first priority is to increase production so that we can exchange goods for goods, which is an active boycotting strategy. Therefore, in terms of the current situation, these two things must be done simultaneously and cannot be neglected. Because if we only boycott without producing, we will still need foreign goods, and the rights and interests will still flow out. The following points can also be used as references:

(1) Leaders of various industries and businesses should take the lead in starting factories, pooling capital, or encouraging capitalists at home and abroad to invest actively. The type of goods to be manufactured should be determined according to the urgency of the need. Existing national goods factories should take this opportunity to find ways to increase production and expand their operations. The government should provide rewards and reduce taxes. For example, in terms of cotton yarn, which is the most needed commodity in the current society, fine yarn of 36 to 42 counts is almost entirely Japanese goods. Now that the supply route has been cut off, there is an urgent need for similar substitutes. Then the China Cotton Yarn Mill Association should convene a meeting to discuss how to add fine yarn equipment and rush to ship goods to meet the urgent demand. If they continue to hesitate, it is simply self-abandonment. Other industries should also convene their peers to cooperate earnestly and eliminate the most despicable mentality of "envy among peers."

(2) Japanese industrial and commercial organizations in Shanghai and other places are trending towards strikes and shutdowns. Our Chinese employees have specialized skills. National goods factories should seize the opportunity to hire them. It is best to organize an agency to handle registration and placement of these people. At the same time, the government and all sectors of society should work together to help solve their livelihood problems after unemployment.

(3) Shanghai should first try to set up a research institution, preferably sponsored by the Anti-Japanese Association. Recruit experienced professionals in industry and commerce. Start with investigations. The types, qualities, prices... of Japanese goods should be accurately statistically analyzed in detail to make various reports for national goods factories to use as a reference. Newly returned industrial and commercial talents from Japan can participate in this work. (4) The Ministry of Industry has long had plans to establish five major factories. Using the country's financial resources to do so is indeed easy to achieve. However, these five major factories are progressing slowly. I don't know when they will be successful. In fact, we Chinese have the raw materials, capital, and talent to run large-scale industries. Unfortunately, there is a lack of enthusiastic advocates.

Now, both Beijing and Guangdong are showing a clear understanding of the greater good. The national plea for "peaceful unification" and Mr. Sun Yat-sen's last words when he was dying, "peaceful unification to save China," can be realized again. However, peaceful unification must also have a permanent guarantee. A virtuous and capable government should also be produced quickly. I hope that our virtuous and capable government will also promulgate a five-year plan to complete the construction of national defense, internal affairs, diplomacy, education, industry and commerce, transportation, etc. according to a specific plan and within a time limit. Revitalizing China and avenging national hatred is the duty of the government. Our 400 million compatriots should work together to promote its realization. Selfishness, dependence, living for the moment, and other inferior character traits are all evident. As a great country, with soldiers, generals, and people, we still think of asking other countries to help when we are being bullied. Even if this is realized, I think it is just adding a second shame of enduring grace on top of the first shame of being bullied. However, most Chinese are actually dreaming that the League of Nations will sanction Japan, or that the United States will send a number of troops to drive the Japanese out of the three northeastern provinces, while we sit idly by and wait to enjoy the fruits. The so-called party-state dignitaries are still enriching themselves and protecting their own power, playing the game of being king among monkeys. Alas, if one has a little self-respect, who can willingly endure this supreme shame? But when China is in danger, it is still filled with this despicable hope.

The Chinese are truly a peaceful people (this sentence is said except when it comes to internal affairs). Instead of saying that they are not competitive, they insist that others are tyrannical. Instead of saying that they are cowardly, they insist that others are barbaric. Moreover, when they are well-fed and have nothing to do, they still loudly sing the tune of world harmony and boast of their brilliance. But who would be willing to "harmonize" with our self-despising, self-deprecating nation and lower their status as a strong country? To be frank, if we want world harmony, it will only be possible when China defeats Japan and also ranks among the major powers. Otherwise, let those Chinese who blindly believe in justice and empty slogans of world harmony cease.

Correction: In the article "Remembering Han Shichang's Martyrdom in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894" the other day, "Han Shichang" was actually a mistake for "Deng Shichang." Deng's descendants, who are famous in the business world, include Deng Junrui, the owner of Deng Zhuang in Hangzhou. We hereby make this correction and thank Mr. Gu Zhipan for pointing it out in his letter.

Novel Club

The Pestle for Knocking on Dreams (3)

— Cheng Zhanlu

"Layman, if China one or two hundred years ago were to appear before your eyes, what would you do?"

"If it were to appear, I would be my peaceful people"; "This place is happy, I don't miss Shu". "It is easy to realize, you only need to sit on this rotating chair". The elder pointed to the chair in the middle and said.

"Old monk, is it true"? Tao Chi chewed on the taro in his mouth, saying vaguely.

"This old monk does not lie. Once the layman sits on the chair, I guarantee that you will realize that dream of a peaceful China in the 18th century."

"Sitting on the chair, can it turn back the years"? Tao Chi said in surprise. "Just turning back the years cannot show the wonderful use of the rotating chair; this rotating chair has three incredible effects: one can make time flow forward, two can make time flow backward, and three can make time stand still". "The old monk's words are too wonderful, please tell me the details".

"Layman, please eat a few more taro, and I will tell you. Time changes with the rotation of the Earth. The Earth is 25,000 miles in circumference and can rotate once in 24 hours; then the speed of the Earth's rotation at the equator should be more than 1,000 miles per hour. China is located in the temperate zone, far from the equator; according to the rule of the Earth's rotation, the farther away from the equator, the slower the rotation speed. Suppose the speed of rotation in our place is 800 miles per hour; once you sit on this rotating chair; the rotation of the wheel is ten million times faster than the Earth's rotation, that is, the Earth rotates 800 miles per hour, and the speed of the rotating wheel is ten million times 800 miles; spending a day on Earth is just passing the hours, but spending a day on the rotating chair has already passed ten million hours. So once you sit on the rotating chair, sitting for an hour, you can see the future history ten million hours later; this is called making time flow forward".

"Please explain how time reversal is explained"?

Gold Exchange Announcement on US Dollar Settlement Price

November Transactions Extended to End of December for Settlement

Yesterday, the Gold Exchange issued two announcements regarding the change to using the US dollar as the standard for settlement prices and the extension of the settlement period. The content is transcribed below: "In response to an official letter from the Shanghai Exchange Supervisor, citing the chaotic foreign exchange market and the need to prevent potential problems, this is to inform you that, given the sharp drop in the British pound and the potential for further fluctuations in other currencies, which would inevitably have an impact, the Exchange convened a board meeting. It was unanimously agreed that the US dollar is considered stable, and physical cash can be transported at any time. Therefore, Article 47 of Chapter 10 of the Business Regulations will be temporarily amended to allow for forward trading. At the end of the period, if the goods have not been fully delivered, the initial exchange rate quoted by HSBC on that day for the US dollar, plus shipping costs, will be used as the standard, with US$240 per tael of standard gold for settlement." This decision was communicated to the Exchange's Brokers Association, which subsequently agreed to implement the change. This announcement serves to inform you that, effective immediately, the amended provisions of the Business Regulations will be implemented accordingly.

Another announcement stated: "Given the distance between China and the United States, it is temporarily necessary to extend the settlement period. Therefore, the transactions already concluded in November will be extended to December 31 as the final settlement deadline. At that time, if the goods have not been fully delivered, the amended provisions of Article 47 of Chapter 10 of the Business Regulations will be applied," and so on.

Silver Dollar Market Atmosphere Calm

Although domestic goods and other imported goods have tried their best to compensate, the people's minds are focused on national salvation, and they are not paying attention to commercial warfare. Therefore, the current business situation in the financial sector is quite dull. The joint resignation of the Chinese compradors of Japanese banks is particularly impactful on the financial sector's quietness.

The cotton yarn market was flat in the morning and rose in the afternoon, with the trend remaining chaotic. The global situation is very pessimistic, and economic sanctions against Japan mean that Japanese yarn cannot be sold, relying instead on Chinese yarn, which is insufficient to supply demand. Therefore, the factories' existing stocks have long been emptied, and market prices have naturally soared. However, the financial situation is bleak, and the floods in all directions are severe, so the price increase may lead to stagnation of current sales. In the afternoon, rumors circulated in the market that Indian merchants were buying in large quantities, which further intensified the rising trend.

The nominal price in the after-market rose by 1 to 2 taels. The nominal price opened flat in the early market. The Spirit of the Children

— Huang Huanruo

This article was written and waiting to be sent when the Japanese bandits

had already launched a large-scale invasion of our eastern province.

Hair stands on end, eyes widen in fury, the whole country shares the same indignation.

I do not know how the children, after receiving this

news, will react with such

indignation.

Because Xue Mei had matters to attend to and could not teach at the school, she asked me to temporarily take over her duties. Thus, the childish me actually ran onto the podium and started acting as "teacher" with gestures. The life of a "Monkey King" is not necessarily as annoying as people curse it to be, sitting on a "cold bench." I have always admired the naturalness and greatness of primary school teachers. If it weren't for a greater mission weighing on my shoulders, perhaps I would also be a small general in the field of primary school education.

The children seemed to have quite good feelings towards me. During class, they listened innocently to my lectures and watched my performances. Even though they instinctively liked to move around, they weren't too noisy. After class, many children gathered around the desk. When taking a walk, many children swarmed around me. The cries of "Teacher," "Teacher," continuously entered my ears, asking questions and eagerly awaiting my replies. This scene was harmonious and beautiful.

The children loved listening to stories the most. Taking advantage of this opportunity, I mixed many supplementary teaching materials into it. Historical stories, enough to cultivate sound national character, were instilled as much as possible, taking this opportunity to achieve a subtle and transformative effect. A certain eugenicist said that China is a hopeless country because the Chinese nation's innate nature is a bad seed. I resolutely oppose this absurd argument. I have always believed that the superiority or inferiority of a nation entirely depends on the level of education. The effect of education is not dead injection, but the subtle influence of the sea. Children love to listen to stories, and educational materials that benefit their minds are the best opportunity for cultivation. When history reached the modern stage, many deeds that could inspire national spirit were left behind. One day, I compiled a story about the historical relationship between China and Japan, preparing to tell it to them. The word "Japan," just mentioning it verbally, even people in remote rural areas would feel anger rising in their hearts. The curse of "dwarf slaves" poured out of the mouths of the people. When the children heard that it would be about the Japanese, everyone expressed their strong agreement. The words "Wanbaoshan Incident" also floated in the children's group.

Starting from how China and Japan came into contact, I talked about the Sino-Japanese War, the Twenty-One Demands, the Wanbaoshan Incident, and finally, the Japanese soldiers' cross-border interference and the inspection work of the anti-Japanese association, and the event of looting goods seized by the anti-Japanese association. The children listened attentively and were unusually excited, but it was somewhat different from peacetime. Smiles were not on their innocent little faces, and their brows were furrowed, obviously, the innocent and peaceful childhood hearts had also been stirred by uneven waves.

"Teacher, then why don't we Chinese go to war with them?" a child asked suspiciously and indignantly.

"Our weapons are not as sophisticated as theirs, not as many as theirs, so we can't win against them," I replied unnaturally.

"Then, we have no hope. We will become slaves to a conquered nation, won't we?" another抢着asked. His body had already stood up from his seat. Dozens of small faces full of suspicion all stared straight at my face, naturally eagerly awaiting my reply.

"That's not necessarily the case. As long as we are willing to strive for self-improvement, we can also become a strong country. However, if we remain unconscious like this forever, then it is really hopeless," I said. I was very happy. The children were not as hopeless as a certain eugenicist said because their enthusiasm fully expressed traces of self-awareness.

"Teacher, if we don't want to be slaves to a conquered nation, do we have to save the country? If we want to save the country, should we boycott Japanese goods?"

"That's right, we want to save the country, we want to boycott Japanese goods. Everyone, do you have any Japanese goods at home? If you don't have any Japanese goods yourselves, I hope you won't buy Japanese goods again in the future," I said to them enthusiastically, and the children were also listening enthusiastically. "Also, in addition to boycotting Japanese goods, don't forget that other foreign goods should also not be bought, unless it is absolutely necessary to use foreign goods. Furthermore, I hope that the children will work hard and sincerely persuade your relatives and friends. From now on, everyone should be affectionate, united, and work together to overcome all difficulties. We should cooperate in all undertakings. Only in this way will foreigners dare not bully us, and only then will China have a prosperous and strong day."

This class ended with excitement and vigor amid the ringing of the bell. The children were not as calm as usual. A kind of patriotic climax of enthusiasm and courage was brewing in the children's group.

The next day, when several of us teachers were taking a walk in the village, we actually saw several children propagating their national salvation policy to the farmers. The farmers also awakened and cursed the Japanese bitterly, nodding their heads in praise of the policies the children were talking about.

In this way, a fervent anti-Japanese atmosphere permeated the entire village.

The spirit of the children is truly extraordinary. Who says that the Chinese nation is hopeless?

Jiaotong University in the Anti-Japanese Voice

— Quan

Jiaotong University has a glorious history in past student movements. In recent years, many talented people have emerged from the school, occupying considerable positions in the engineering and scientific fields. The school authorities' cultivation efforts and patriotic movements have also had an impact. This time, when news of the Japanese's atrocities arrived, the student union's representative assembly of the school held several temporary emergency meetings and resolved to convene a general assembly to discuss ways to save the country. All students attended the meeting, crowded and respectful, setting a record never seen before. After the chairman reported on the Japanese atrocities, the atmosphere in the entire venue suddenly became tragic. Some covered their faces and wept, while others cried out loud. At that time, the entire body resolved to immediately organize an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee to handle the following matters:

(1) Military Training: The school's military training was originally strict. Students were fully armed with live ammunition, practicing twice a week. The results were quite remarkable. Last time, the directorate of training inspected the school and was amazed. It was commended by an order from the ministry. Now that foreign aggression is imminent, students should urgently use armed force to save the country. Special military training is being intensified. All students who are not scheduled to lecture must practice for four hours every day, teach for two hours, and camp out in tents at night, and practice field warfare situations, so that students can have sufficient military knowledge when they serve on the battlefield in the future and fight the Japanese.

(2) Military Chemistry: Xu Mingcai, a chemistry professor at the school, was originally the chief engineer of the Hanyang Arsenal and has in-depth research on military chemistry. Now, he is specially adding more research hours, burying himself in the laboratory, preparing to research a kind of (Mustard Gas Cl·C2H4·C2H4Cl·) for wartime use, hoping to succeed by June to help him in his research is the famous chemist Zhang Huaiyi.

Youth Garden Manuscript Rules

(1) The text should be related to the discussion of youth issues, domestic and foreign school or student news, essays, school life descriptions, etc., the style is not limited.

(2) Limited to matters relating to youth issues.

(3) Photos should be related to youth life (such as sports, travel, viewing, relief, gatherings, exhibitions and various competitions), school news, and youth movement. Whether it is individual photos or group photos, all are welcome. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(4) The number of words per text should not exceed two thousand.

Social News

Aviation in Malaya Qiu Bin Cun (Continued)

There are other airfields that are under construction. After the completion of various aircraft fields in the Malay Peninsula in the future, not only will mail delivery be faster, but passenger air travel can also be achieved.

Conclusion

My conclusion is that when the Malay airfields are scattered like stars and extremely meticulous, not only will the postal and transportation affairs of Malaya itself have considerable development, but the economy and culture of Europe, Africa, Asia, and Australia will also have amazing progress. This kind of statement is observed from its good aspects. If we observe from its bad aspects, the world economy is trapped in the dangerous cliff of depression. The United Kingdom is still desperately developing British and Australian aviation, then its other intentions can be known. Because the British colony spans Europe, Africa, Asia, and Australia, if there is no sensitive military force as a guarantee, there is a danger of losing it everywhere. Its intention to build a military port in Singapore and develop British and Australian aviation is nothing more than to obtain military contact, so as to permanently retain its acquired territories and rights and interests. Therefore, on the day when Malayan aviation is fully developed, the United Kingdom will be like a tiger with wings added, and its position in Europe, Africa, Asia, and Australia, especially in the Far East, will be as stable as Mount Tai and cannot be shaken. (End)

Japan's Insidious Means of Dealing with Northeast附属Territories Qiu Yao Min

The outbreak of Japanese imperialism's armed invasion of China this time is not an accidental move, but has its profound basis. We only need to observe his usual management of the Northeast, and we can get a general view. Last year, I went to the Northeast because of something, and I personally saw and heard all kinds of insidious and rigid means used by Japanese imperialism to deal with the local subordinate people. Now, I will list them as follows. From this, we can probably see the determination of Japanese imperialists to meticulously manage the Northeast and their actions of seizing land and killing people this time.

(1) Openly Establishing Opium Retail Stores Opium retail stores are not only densely packed in urban areas (such as Dalian Toutaogou...), but also everywhere in rural and remote areas. For example, in Dengshahe, a very small rural area, there are two publicly sold opium stores. There are countless in Dalian. There are probably no less than seventy or eighty stores in Changchun Toutaogou. According to the investigation of the Taidong Bao, the total income of opium retail stores in Dalian alone reaches more than 4,000 yuan per day. If we try to enter these opium retail stores, we can see countless compatriots swallowing clouds and spitting fog, "a lifetime career of happiness (?) lantern flowers," and not caring about anything. Not only

Page 22

this, the most vicious morphine, heroin... are also sold everywhere, and are popularized to the most miserable people. Therefore, the brains of our compatriots are numb, and they are more easily ruled. (2) Giving small favors to win over the people The most vicious and insidious means of the Japanese in treating the people of the leased territories is to give small favors. Because of this, ordinary people with dim minds and narrow vision will sing praises to them and tend to them. For example, teaching people how to grow cotton and providing medical treatment... they do not hesitate to spend a lot of money and do their best. Once, I personally saw two or three Japanese people pruning apple tree branches for the people "free of charge" in an apple orchard in the countryside. At that time, heavy rain was imminent, and the common people who were listening to him lecture on plant physiology all slipped away, while these few Japanese people who loved the people like their own children (?) still worked in the rain. How can you not be impressed?

(3) Forcibly Buying Land On the one hand, Japanese imperialists use insidious and soft means, but on the other hand, they do not hesitate to reveal their ferocious faces. Now, their barbarous and forceful means, such as forcibly buying land, are the most important examples. It is said that the land is forcibly bought at the price stipulated by their Kwantung Office 丨 the lowest price.

The above is just a few of them. The rest, such as schools, rural self-government associations... are all scheming and fighting, doing their best to fulfill their instinct to invade.

Now they are coming in a big way. They not only want to manage the leased territories, they want to seize our three northeastern provinces, they want to destroy our entire country. Arise, arm yourself and expel Japanese imperialists, and recover the leased territories.

French General Foch's Diary of the European War Gu Ang Ruo, translated

The Allied General Offensive, October 15 to November 11, 1918

The Allied forces advanced between the North Sea and the Meuse River, with a front of two hundred miles, attacking in separate directions, naturally avoiding encountering formidable enemies in several places. It is difficult to predict the extent of the enemy's resistance. Only by studying the terrain in front of each army and the speed of each army's advance can we know a little. But in general, the Allied forces from right to left, that is, from the mountainous area on both sides of the Meuse River to the great plains of France, the terrain is lower and flatter. From ancient times to Waterloo, the fate of Europe was often decided there.

In the area north of the Aisne River, our army can most easily use its superior forces. The most important advantage in modern times is that our army's equipment and ammunition supply exceed the enemy's. The astonishing progress made by the British army here is clear evidence of this. Continuing to advance is also obviously beneficial. Moreover, with the influence of our army's separate attacks, the blow suffered by the enemy in one place will inevitably affect other places. Therefore, although other places are still sufficient to resist, they are also affected and shaken.

On October 10, I asked Marshal Haig to pay attention to this situation. At the same time, I ordered Commander Petain to reinforce the French First Army on the right wing of the British army. The content of my instruction is as follows:

Today, October 10, the direction of the three-way meeting of troops is as follows: (1) Belgian side, (2) along the Charleroi-Wasigny line, (3) along the Aisne-Meuse line. Because of the British army's victory, the most advantageous for offensive is the Charleroi-Wasigny line, so the battle should be carried out with all its strength. In this way, not only can we go directly to Mons and Avesnes, but we can also develop the following plan: (A) Join the attack on the Belgian side to clear the Lille area, which will be undertaken by the British army, fighting northeast between the Scheldt River and the Scarpe River. The scope of operations between the British and French armies extends to the south of Wasigny and the south of Avesnes, so that the British army's attack can develop northward.

(B) Join the attack on the Aisne-Meuse line, with the Selle River line, which will be undertaken by the French First Army. The first batch of reinforcements will be transferred to the First Army to help in the battle. The reinforcements that arrive later will be transferred to the Belgian side or the Aisne-Meuse line to help in the battle.

On October 15, the French and American armies between the Aisne River and the Argonne Forest went straight to Mézières, encountering the German army's strong defense line (Tingding斯特朗 and 布朗希爾特斯特朗 line,) which started from拉發爾, passed 克萊西西沙伏齊歐 all the way to 格倫特普爾,

North of the Aisne River, the British army attacked Mons Avesnes, advancing to the Wasigny·勒加篤·沙勒斯美·杜亞意 line on the same day. The army shook the Lille area from the south, and the French army group between the Lys River and the North Sea threatened from the north. The army group had reached a stable position on October 14. There is no concern about transportation. It had already resumed its offensive between Steen and Wervicq, and the situation was very favorable. The American army withdrawn from the front line had also been transferred to help in the battle. Furthermore, because the French army in that area increased, General Pousoudy was sent to serve as commander of the Sixth Army, and General De Cointet remained as the chief of staff of the Belgian king, assisting the Belgian king in commanding the battle.

After the French army group was supplemented in this way, it continued to attack straight to Thourout·谷特萊·和蒙明, developing rapidly, occupying賀爾特魯勒 and 摩西爾 on the 14th, attacking past谷特馬克 on the 15th, advancing to the city of 谷特萊 , attacking into蒙明 and 瓦活克, 韜樂·列希特韋爾特·亞杜意·伊斯堪 were captured one after another on the 16th. The enemy army then withdrew from the entire Belgian coast, and all coastal batteries and submarine bases that had endangered British and British-French transportation for several years were also abandoned.

On the 17th, the Belgian army recovered 奥斯敦, on the 19th, it recovered布倫肯堡 and 齊布魯治, on the 20th, the Belgian army advanced to the Dutch border and the希普同運河, and King Albert of Belgium was also preparing to re-enter Bruges in triumph.

The plan decided by the Allied Commander-in-Chief five weeks ago to "defeat the enemy army in Belgian territory and recover the lost land north of the Lys River" has now been completed by the French army group.

On October 22, I personally congratulated the Belgian army, and notified them to reorganize their teams, restore transportation, contact the rear, and arrange for the marines along the coast to respond, and then immediately continue to advance.

While the French army group was advancing between the North Sea and the Lys River, the right wing of the British army also continued to attack in the direction of Wasigny and Charleroi according to plan. On October 17, the British Fourth Army broke through the enemy's stubborn resistance and occupied勒加篤. On the 18th and 19th, it occupied Wasigny and Charleroi, driving the German army back to the east bank of the Sambre Aisne Lien River. The right wing and the British Third Army contacted and crossed the Selle River, occupying Charleroi (October 20), and advanced to蘭特勒西 and摩麻爾林邊 (October 24). On the left wing, the British Third Army cleared the south bank of the Sanshi River, attacked across the愛加宏河, and advanced to勒格斯諾 and the city of凡倫西 (October 24 and 26).

In the northern battle, the French army group was the left road and the right wing of the British army was the right road, advancing side by side. At the same time, the British First and Fifth Armies were responsible for the middle road, pressing the enemy army on the front, and causing the enemy army to implement a general retreat. The enemy army's front line began to retreat from the Lys River to the史家坡河 on October 17. After ten days, on October 17, our army recovered 列藜 and 杜亞意, on the 18th, it recovered 馬爾興 and 巴興, on the 20th, it recovered 特宗, on the 21st, it recovered 聖亞蒙, and on the 27th, the British army advanced to the left bank of the 希爾特河 across the entire line, and 都那義 to 凡倫西 were all recovered. The right wing of the French army group re-attacked, crossed the Lys River, occupied 谷拉義 on October 19, and immediately continued to advance to the 希爾特河, reaching the river bank between 亞夫爾 and 都那義 (October 20 to 26). The left wing and middle road of the French army group took advantage of the victory and attacked again on October 31, fighting fiercely for four days, driving the enemy army back to the right bank of the 希爾特河, and the military plan of October 10 was developed to the north of the Aisne River.

I was able to continue to advance the right wing army towards the common goal of Mézières on October 19, and also transfer troops to develop new targets.

My plan is as follows:
